Current Commentary

Commemorating Confucius 70

— Heng

The 123rd Central Standing Committee resolved to designate today as a "National Memorial Day" to commemorate the birth of Confucius. We cannot help but have some thoughts on this. Let us try to elaborate on them.

The main factors constituting a nation, besides a common language and writing system, should be its common history. And within history, what can most deeply imprint itself on people's minds and linger there are the great figures and their words and deeds. The English often boast to the world about having a Shakespeare. The Germans also pride themselves on being the most cultured nation because they have Kant and others. This is not to say that transcendent personalities can truly be unprecedented and unparalleled, illuminating the ages. Rather, it is to use the greatness of the nation's past to awaken its confidence for the future, enabling it to carry on the past and forge ahead to compete in today's world. Precisely because of this, even though Ireland has been merged with England for hundreds of years, in order to maintain its independent existence and develop its future national destiny, it still strives to restore its inherent culture and promote its inherent history, thereby continuing its interrupted historical sentiment and extending its severed national feelings. Compared with any other country in the world, our country's past was characterized by splendid culture, a long history, and numerous great figures. There is absolutely nothing to be ashamed of. Today, as the nation's power declines, faced with foreign aggression, and with national sentiments scattered to the extreme, selecting one or two great figures in history worthy of worship and commemorating them regularly to boost the nation's demoralized spirit and enable it to be bold and proactive is a necessary measure. And the authorities' choice of Confucius seems to have even deeper meaning.

Confucius is the most worthy of worship of all the great figures in our country's history. This is an undeniable fact. Recent commentators often say that during the Zhou and Qin periods, a hundred schools of thought contended, and there were many astonishing and valuable academic achievements. Yet, from the Han dynasty onwards, only Confucius was revered as the sole authority, remaining so for thousands of years. The reason for this is that Confucius's doctrines aligned with the psychology of emperors, and thus he was revered by emperors of all dynasties. There is some truth to this. However, to say that Confucius was revered solely for this reason is not only to belittle Confucius's personality but also to turn those who worship him into unconscious, blind human beings. The falsity of this claim cannot be concealed.

We believe that Confucius is revered for several reasons: (1) his personal character; (2) his proposals for saving the world; (3) his attitude of "not compromising"; and (4) his teachings on life. What was Confucius's personal character like? No one knows better than his disciples. Confucius lived in a chaotic world. He was not successful in Lu and was not accepted in Wei. He was also trapped between Chen and Cai, wandering for fourteen years and ultimately unable to realize his ambitions. However, during these times of hardship, his disciples' devotion to Confucius did not diminish in the slightest. Zilu even wanted to follow Confucius to "float on the sea on a raft." Zigong also said, "The Master's Way is great, therefore the world cannot contain it." Never did their sincerity of belief diminish due to Confucius's lack of success. How could this be achieved without the power of his personal influence? And after Confucius passed away, his disciples all observed mourning for three years, along with three years of mourning in their hearts. Zigong even built a hut and lived alone by his grave for six years. More than a hundred other disciples moved to live near the grave, eventually forming the Confucius Village of later generations. All these facts cannot be explained solely based on the reverence of later emperors.

Furthermore, Confucius's political proposals were also a reason for his being revered by later generations. Confucius lived when the Zhou dynasty had already declined. The feudal lords invaded each other, wars were frequent, and the people suffered. Confucius's political proposals at that time were to practice the Way of Kings and reject deception and force. He even disagreed with Guan Zhong's actions of "uniting the feudal lords nine times and rectifying the world," saying that Guan Zhong could only make Qi a hegemon, not a king. Therefore, Confucius's intention was to prioritize the unification of China. If unification could be achieved, then it would not be necessary to repeatedly revere the Zhou dynasty, whose national fortune had already declined. From Confucius's traveling among the states to seek to serve the world, it can be seen that his ambition was truly to have any state become king of the world, and not to revere the Zhou dynasty. Therefore, it is said, "If someone were to employ me, I could accomplish something in a month, and in three years there would be success." Is this why Confucius became a "sage of the times"? What Confucius sought was a unified China, and his method was the Way of Kings, which refused to "kill one innocent person to gain the world." Therefore, he said, "If distant people do not submit, then cultivate virtue to attract them." Confucius's proposals at the time were not only to seek the unification of China but also to seek the abolition of civil war in China.

A third aspect worthy of our reverence is that although Confucius was restless and anxious in seeking to serve the world, he would serve if he could implement his proposals, and he would retreat if he could not implement his proposals, without any lingering attachment. Therefore, when Confucius was the minister of Lu, as soon as Ji Huanzi indulged in the Qi female musicians and neglected state affairs, he left Lu for other places. Thereafter, he traveled among the states, using the ability to implement his proposals as the principle for advancing or retreating. It can be seen that Confucius was truly a statesman with proposals, not a politician who only knew how to seek wealth and status. Therefore, it is said, "Wealth and honor obtained through unrighteousness are like floating clouds to me."

As for the cultivation of life, the teachings valued by the ancients, none surpass those of Confucius. There is no need to discuss this in depth. From these few points, it is clear that Confucius is the greatest figure in Chinese history. His worthiness of our reverence and commemoration is also self-evident. However, what we cannot help but say is that although Confucius's character is great, his thought cannot escape the limitations of his time. The most obvious example is the policy of the Way of Kings, which emphasizes benevolence and righteousness and rejects force. It is very good to implement this within China, but it will certainly have no effect on the international stage, where the weak are prey to the strong. This is one point. Furthermore, Confucius's political ideal is a monarchical polity, which is not without conflict with the current system of the Republic of China. This is what we must pay special attention to when the authorities commemorate Confucius. In short, the thought of any great figure cannot escape the limitations of their time. Therefore, our worship must be rational worship, not blind worship. Furthermore, the key to our worship of great figures lies not in simply praising the ancients but in having the confidence to "see the worthy and think of emulating them."

German Propaganda Campaign to Reclaim the Saar 71

Demonstration Held in Koblenz

140,000 People Submit Oaths of Loyalty to Hitler

(Koblenz) Today, people from the Saar and various parts of Germany came to Koblenz in an endless stream to participate in the massive Saar declaration of loyalty demonstration. Hitler and von Papen will both speak tomorrow to proclaim to the masses. The houses in the city are almost entirely filled with National Socialists. Imperial flags can be seen everywhere. There are currently more than 200 special trains transporting participants to the demonstration. These people will march from 6 a.m. tomorrow to the Ehrenbreitstein Fortress opposite Koblenz and gather in the square. In the past five days, 140,000 people have relayed oaths of loyalty from all parts of the country to the Saar. The oath from Rügen Island in Pomerania, across the Strelasund, was carried to the mainland by swimmers. The oath from Helgoland was carried by sailboat. The oath from the summit of the Zugspitze in Bavaria was carried down by mountain climbing experts. All oaths will be presented to Hitler at the demonstration. After the demonstration, 10,000 carrier pigeons will be released, followed by a bonfire and the lighting of lamps. The fortress was besieged by French troops in 1623 and 1688 without being taken. It was finally captured in 1799. After the Treaty of Lunéville, it was demolished. It was rebuilt by the Prussian government in 1816. (25th Reuters)

(Berlin) Today, a large-scale propaganda campaign will be held near Koblenz at Ehrenbreitstein to demand that the Saar region be returned to Germany. Hitler, the "Leader and Chancellor," will personally participate and deliver a speech. This morning, German newspapers harshly criticized France's policies in the Saar region and the Saar Administrative Commission. The local newspaper stated, "The Saar region has suffered for fifteen years and will now return to Germany." The newspaper's wording was particularly harsh in its attacks on the League of Nations. The Catholic Party's Germania newspaper stated that if the Saar region's governance system remains as it is, it would be no different from being incorporated into France. Opponents of Hitler and advocates for maintaining the status quo in Saarbrücken demonstrated separately yesterday. Sympathizers of the National Socialist Party traveled to Koblenz by special train to participate in the "Movement to Return the Saar to Germany." The round-trip fare was originally 120 francs, but it was specially reduced to 20 francs. Several thousand unemployed people were also able to travel for free. (26th Havas)

Artificial Rain Experiment Successful 76

Bombs Dropped at High Altitude

Clouds Condense into Rain Upon Encountering Cold

(Walker, CA, USA) An artificial rain experiment conducted here today using scientific methods has been completely successful. Chemist Botz and aviator Borden flew to an altitude of 15,000 feet and dropped a small steel cannon containing a bomb into the clouds 5,000 feet below. According to scientific principles, the bomb can generate cold air, causing the clouds to condense into rain. The residents here, who had been hoping for rain, were rewarded with rain within fifteen minutes. However, it was only temporary and not enough to stop the dust from flying. They plan to conduct another experiment next week, using a bomb with a hundred times more power. They believe that the method has been found, but further testing is needed to create rain in a larger area. (25th National Telegram)

The Actual Economic Situation in Japan (Japanese Correspondence) 81

Sericulture Plummets, Silk withers.

Rural Areas Decline, Farmers Suffer.

- Saitama Prefecture as an Example -

The so-called "prosperity" of Japanese society in general is actually a volatile "prosperity." Dumping exports and military industries are acts of "swelling the face to look fat." They do not greatly benefit the actual economic market. Although the Mitsubishi Economic Research Institute's survey of Japan's major industrial production indexes shows an increase, except for the raw silk industry, cotton yarn and cotton cloth can barely maintain a balance. Industries related to military affairs, such as coal, pig iron, steel manufacturing, and the chemical industry, are constantly increasing. Japanese industrial capitalists, especially the military clique, boast that the current economic situation is no less than that of the Soviet Union and has surpassed that of European and American countries. Therefore, they are striving to open up markets on the one hand and actively preparing for war on the other.

However, the facts show that the optimistic materials mentioned above are only a one-sided picture of brightness. Nowadays, in the cities, one cannot help but hear sighs about the difficulty of finding work, and hungry vagrants can be seen everywhere. In particular, since the spring cocoons were put on the market this year, silk prices have plummeted, falling to almost the same level as in 1932. The future is even worse than before because the manufacturing of rayon is becoming increasingly sophisticated, gradually taking over the market for raw silk. Furthermore, because the American market is still sluggish, such luxury goods will inevitably be the first to suffer. Therefore, Japanese raw silk exports are encountering rare misfortune.

Originally, Japan's rural economy had already encountered problems. The problem is overproduction. If rice prices fall, farmers are extremely distressed. The drop in cocoon prices makes income from sideline businesses equivalent to zero. Over the years, the total debt accumulated by rural villages across Japan amounts to as much as seven billion yen. Since 1930, it has been in a state of being frozen. Although there was a slight tendency to improve last year, this year's drought and floods have been significant and widespread, along with the following signs:

(1) This year's spring cocoon prices are low, similar to the year before. However, the summer and autumn cocoons of the year before gradually recovered their old prices. There is little hope for this year.

(2) Currently, rice prices are quite high. It is still unpredictable what will happen after the new rice comes onto the market. The only concern is that the climate this year is unfavorable. No matter what, there will be a reduction in the harvest. Even if rice prices rise, it will be a losing proposition.

(3) Rural fatigue is a chronic disease accumulated over many years. Currently, there are not only no fundamental solutions, but also the temporary mitigation measures are still unbearable for farmers. Moreover, whether the so-called rural countermeasures of the current Okada government can be effectively implemented is a big question. The deterioration of the rural situation is very worrying.

The above three situations are crises commonly acknowledged by Japanese society in general, and it is believed that they will inevitably affect the entire society. For example, the total debt of rural villages in Nagano Prefecture alone amounts to 250 million yuan. In fact, there is no other way but to postpone repayment. However, the Hypothec Bank of Japan and other financial institutions are pressured by the market's decline and cannot but pursue the repayment of debts. It is truly difficult to find a solution to this situation.

Another example is the famous Chichibu Town in Saitama Prefecture, a neighboring prefecture of Tokyo Prefecture, and Urayama Village, about nine miles away. Considering the location, it can be regarded as being at the foot of the emperor, a land of fish and rice. Although the transportation is not very convenient, it used to retain some primitive vestiges, a society of female rights. The words of a housewife were worth a thousand gold, and her "powers" were far greater than those of men. This is something rarely seen in Japan. However, recently, among the more than 250 households in Urayama Village, there are only three sick women who are virgins. The rest have abandoned their happiness and left the village to find hard labor because there is really no way to survive in the village. The rice harvested last year has been sold out. The money earned from selling cocoons this year is not enough to cover the costs, so there is no money to buy rice to eat. Most elementary school children cannot eat their fill. Many people have no rice to eat, and some even eat grass roots. For weddings, only two or three close relatives can be invited. There is absolutely no strength to entertain other guests. During the banquet, everyone drinks three cups as a token of good wishes, and there is no more wine to drink. Charcoal is produced in Mount Bukō in the area. Workers earn only eight yuan a month, but they have to support a family of five or six people. Each person earns only four or five sen (less than five cents in silver) per day. Therefore, elementary school children also take advantage of their summer vacation to carry charcoal in the mountains. They carry a bag of charcoal from the top of the mountain to the bottom, earning only three sen. Each child can earn twelve to eighteen sen per day. The predicament can be imagined. This village was not a particularly poor village in the past, but now it has become such a sight. There are many such places throughout Japan. In this situation, can it be said that it is not serious? (August 21, Tokyo)

Japan Intensifies War Preparations Against Russia in the Northeast 82

= Active Military Action =

= The Soviet Union Responds Tightly =

Harbin Correspondence: Recently, the Japanese army, due to the breakdown of negotiations with the Soviet puppet over the Chinese Eastern Railway, is actively making military arrangements in the Northeast. The Soviet Union is also making equal military preparations. The fellow countrymen in the Northeast, viewing this tense situation, with the pain of a lost province and the disaster of war, are panicked, as if a major catastrophe is about to come. The following is an exploration of the situation:

(Japanese Military Deployment) Recently, the situation in the Northeast between Japan and Russia has become increasingly tense. The Russian side is not only working hard to prepare for defense against Japan but also sending Communist Party members to the countryside to conduct anti-Japanese propaganda. The Japanese are building a large number of barracks and airfields along the major stations of the South Manchurian Railway. To the east of Gongzhuling Street, large barracks, arsenals, and marching headquarters have been built. To the north of the street, large airfields and bomb factories are being built. The project is extremely large, and thousands of workers are actively working on it. It is also rumored that Japanese-Russian military action will break out after the breakdown of negotiations on the "transfer" of the Chinese Eastern Railway. Wealthy families and merchants with sufficient capital here are all remitting money to Guan Nei (China proper) to avoid the ravages of war. This shows the degree of the swaying of the people's hearts. The strength of the Japanese army deployed in the Northeast and the recent state of its military equipment are listed below: (1) Two Japanese divisions are stationed in Suifenhe and Mudanjiang. The marching plan is to use Suifenhe as the first line of defense and Mudanjiang as the second line of defense. (2) Four Japanese divisions are stationed in Heihe and Longmen County, with Heihe as the first line of defense and Longmen County as the second line of defense. (3) Two Japanese divisions are stationed in Manzhouli and Hailar, and the main force seems to be strengthening Longmen. In addition, regarding the deployment of river defenses, a total of more than 30 defensive ships are gathered on the Songhua River, Heilongjiang River, and Ussuri River. Each ship is equipped with anti-aircraft installations (such as searchlights, anti-aircraft machine guns, and anti-aircraft guns). At the same time, one ship is carrying eight aircraft, currently docked at Xizhengyang River in Harbin. It is also heard that the Japanese fleet anchored in Shanghai will return to Lushun and Dalian in early September to strengthen its military strength in the Northeast. Furthermore, the Japanese army is paying particular attention to the transportation for marching. According to reports, between Lushun, Shenyang, Qiqihar, and Heihe, there is currently only a gap of 200 li that has not been connected by railway. Therefore, an extremely strong automobile road has been built in this section to facilitate military action. The Japanese also plan to build a military railway from Tumen River, through Yanji, Dongmi, and directly to Tongjiang, which will be planned and started soon.

The Japanese army has also set up an airfield at the former site of the Jiaotong Middle School in Siping Street, stationed with more than a hundred Japanese soldiers. In Bamiancheng, to the west of the railway station, a barracks has also been built that can accommodate more than 2,000 people. Currently, about several hundred Japanese soldiers are stationed there. The Japanese army has also built a large barracks to the north of the consulate on the west side of Liaoyuan County Railway Station, which can accommodate more than 3,000 people. Currently, about 400 Japanese soldiers are stationed there. There is an airfield to the east of the station where planes can land and refuel. A barracks has been built in Kaitong County, which can accommodate 500 people. The 4th Cavalry Brigade of the Japanese army and a squadron of aircraft are stationed in Taonan County. Recently, the Japanese army has purchased high-rise houses in the city and built a large barracks that can accommodate thousands of people. This place is the most important, and there are more Japanese troops stationed here. Baichengzi is located to the north of Taonan and is the starting point of the Tao-Suo Railway. The Japanese have built a large barracks and a large airfield here, each capable of accommodating a division. The situation here is very important for the connection between Outer Mongolia and "North Manchuria." Therefore, the Japanese military deployment here is quite complete. The Japanese closely monitor the residents in this area. All correspondence is subject to thorough investigation by the Japanese. Residents are often searched by Japanese military police and puppet police, and there is a risk of residents being arrested or harmed. Therefore, the people of Liaobei are extremely agitated and mostly join the work of the volunteer army.

(Russian Preparations) The Soviet Union, in view of Japan's eagerness to prepare for war, is also striving to strengthen its defensive equipment in the Far East. According to recent reliable intelligence, the Soviet Union has gathered 150,000 troops in the Heihe area, about 50,000 elite troops west of Suifenhe, and more than 70,000 Chinese and Korean volunteer soldiers. There are a total of 100,000 Red Army soldiers in the Manzhouli area. Solid fortifications have been built between Manzhouli and Suifenhe. More than 100 Russian planes practice in the airspace on the Northeast border every day. In addition, 60 to 70% of the volunteer armies east of Harbin also receive economic assistance from the Russian side, as well as a small number of new weapons. The most powerful of these is Zhao Shangzhi, who is currently in Bin County and enjoys the support of the people. In addition, similar volunteer armies also appear from time to time in the areas along the lower reaches of the river and the Harbin-Suifenhe line. According to the above situation, the Soviet Union not only has a strong military force of its own but also has the assistance of a large number of Chinese and Korean volunteer armies. Although Japan is actively plotting to attack the Soviet Union, it seems to have some concerns.

According to information from a certain party, in order to prepare for war against Japan and disrupt the Japanese army's rear, the Soviet Union has formed so-called suicide squads composed of Chinese, Russian, and Korean laborers and sent them to various parts of Manchuria. Li Qieou has now been appointed as the commander to form the suicide squads. It is heard that the Soviet Union first provides the suicide squads with six months of training in assassination, bomb use, and other methods, and then sends them to Manchuria to carry out activities.

Japanese Merchants in Java Oppose the Dutch East Indies 83

Ceramic Restriction Law

Japanese Merchants Declare a Strong Stance

Resisting by Suspending Exports

Batavia Special Dispatch: The Dutch-Japanese Conference is on the verge of collapse due to the implementation of the ceramic restriction law in the Dutch East Indies. Since both sides are still arranging their positions, hoping to make a final struggle, there has been no major development so far. At present, in addition to the Japanese Minister to the Netherlands, Takeyoshi Muto, negotiating with the Dutch Foreign Minister, Dirk de Graeff, the Japanese Foreign Minister, Koki Hirota, is also consulting with the Dutch Minister to Japan, Aart van Brienen. Therefore, it is still difficult to predict the outcome. However, all Japanese expatriates in the Dutch East Indies are extremely indignant about this. Japanese newspapers are strongly attacking the Dutch East Indies government's actions, calling them "atrocities" and "oppression." The representatives of Japan attending the Dutch-Japanese Conference have also made up their minds that if the Dutch side does not abolish this restriction law, the Dutch-Japanese Conference will have no other way to go except to break down. As for the Japanese merchants in the Dutch East Indies, they have also united. It is said that their purpose is to encourage the Japanese government and Japanese representatives to resist the measures of the Dutch East Indies government. Recently, seven major Japanese business groups in Java issued a statement, which reads: The Java Ceramic Importers Association was initiated by Japanese merchants, and Chinese merchants gladly participated. The four major Dutch merchants had originally agreed to join, but when the Dutch-Japanese Conference started, they overturned the previous agreement and suddenly announced that they refused to participate. The Dutch East Indies government, under the pretext of stabilizing the market and promoting coexistence and co-prosperity between Japan and the Netherlands, and this importers association, issued an import restriction order for this commodity. This is a misinterpretation of the people's cooperation. Moreover, the issuance of this restriction order is actually the prelude to the full implementation of the restriction orders for 56 commodities in the Dutch East Indies. Therefore, whether the Dutch-Japanese Conference can succeed depends on whether this restriction order can be revoked. (Omission) Now, the Japanese government is doing its best to revoke this restriction order. In order to support the government's measures and promote the resolution of this case by the Japan Ceramic Exporters Association Federation, we advocate prohibiting exports to Java to promote the Dutch East Indies' reflection. This is a necessary and urgent matter, and we hope that they can adopt our opinions. The signatories are the All-Java Japanese Miscellaneous Goods Importers Association League, the All-Java Japanese Retailers Association League, the Surabaya Business Association, the Batavia Business Association, the Semarang Business Association, the Bandung Business Association, and the Java Ceramic Importers Association and other groups.

The Batavia Japanese Business Association held a meeting because the Dutch East Indies government adopted high-pressure tactics against Japan. The main points of its resolutions are as follows: This restriction order of the Dutch East Indies government is not just a single problem of ceramics. If this restriction order is not revoked, then other restrictions will inevitably be implemented one after another in the future. Therefore, this matter must be fought for.

At the same time, the Surabaya Japanese Business Association also decided to take the same attitude and sent a telegram to the Japanese Minister of Commerce and Industry, with quite strong wording. The main points of the telegram are as follows: Regarding the Dutch East Indies government's attempt to exclude Japanese goods and the revocation of the anti-Japanese goods order, we trust the plenipotentiary representatives to expect their results. Now, the Dutch East Indies government suddenly issued a discriminatory law on the import of ceramics. Regarding the immediate revocation of the violent law, we believe that the plenipotentiary representatives will take urgent measures. In order to protect the rights of Japanese merchants, we are willing to sacrifice everything and decided to suspend business. We hope that merchants in Japan will immediately stop exporting before the revocation of this restriction law. The outcome of this matter will be a touchstone for various commodities in the future. If this unity fails this time, it will be taken advantage of by the Dutch East Indies. It will be difficult to protect the rights of Japanese merchants thereafter. Judging from the attitudes of the Japanese merchants in the above two places, the intensity of Japan's opposition to the ceramic restriction law promulgated by the Dutch East Indies government this time can be seen. However, their weapons of opposition are "embargo" and "not selling." This kind of method, whether it can make the Dutch side yield, although the Japanese merchants have this confidence, it is difficult to be optimistic from our perspective. The ceramic products imported into the Dutch East Indies are not only from Japan. Even if Japanese merchants in the Dutch East Indies can prohibit the import of their own country's ceramic products into the Dutch East Indies, how can they prohibit the import of ceramic products from other countries?

Yu and Yellow Qinhai River Project 84

Chen Ruzhen's Inspection Report

Kaifeng Correspondence: Chen Ruzhen, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, crossed the river from Taoyuankou on the morning of the 16th with Tao, a technician, to inspect the recent situation of the Yellow River's north bank and the Qinhai River project. He returned to Bian yesterday morning. The following is a record of his report: "Yellow River" (1) In the northern flood of Kaifeng, the top of the No. 3 dam of the 19th fort was heavily eroded. It collapsed two zhang (approximately 6.6 meters) on the 13th of this month. Stones are being thrown to extend it. Fortunately, the tip of the second spur has not sunk below the water surface. Stones have been thrown on it together with the collapsed parts of the fifth and sixth spurs to resist the water. However, it is difficult to obtain soil in this flood area. The top surface of the levee has been raised by about one meter this time. With the recent sharp rise in water, a sub-levee has been built on the side facing the river, which is one meter higher than the new levee. The entire flood area has been completed by 80%. There will be no danger even if the water rises again in the future. (2) In the northern flood of Kai-Chen, from the 20th fort of the northern flood of Kaifeng to the 2nd fort of this flood area, all the dams are made of stone. There has been no erosion after this flood. However, on the levee surface of the 1st to 3rd forts, after heavy rain, many flood nests were found, and there was also a large nest spanning the levee. Workers have been hired to fill them. The levees below the 2nd fort are all level ground. The levee north of this flood area is low, and the land is mostly saline-alkali. During the last flood, the area below Xibatou was already overflowing due to the lack of levees. Fortunately, the overflowing water carried silt and did not cause great harm. (3) The Yang, Feng, Yuanyang, and Wu Rong flood areas are all level ground. The maintenance and construction of the dikes are still good this time. (4) In the Wuzhi flood area, the main stream eroded the levee near Fangling. Stones have been thrown to protect it, so there is no need to worry. The 9th and 12th dams of the 9th fort collapsed by 4 zhang on the 10th. New stones were used day and night to protect it. As of the 17th, more than 3,000 cubic meters of stone have been thrown. The dam is directly facing the connecting gully, and the downstream swift current is directly hitting it. If the new stones were not sufficient, it would not have been protected. The area above and below the mouth of the Qin River is extremely dangerous and unimaginable. The new levee north of the two Yan Villages under Jiabu was heavily eroded by the main stream. The levee collapsed by more than 30 zhang. More than 6,000 willows were planted on the 16th, and two stone spurs were thrown. It is not very safe. An order was issued to send workers to throw stones to protect the levee foundation. "Qin River" (1) In the Renxiao Temple and Zhongxian Xubao projects, there was erosion between the old levees in Renxiao and Zhongxian. They are being reinforced. The current in Xubao is approaching the levee, and the old levee has been eroded. Fortunately, the project still has materials in reserve. An order was issued to quickly reinforce it to avoid further collapse. (2) The Shantai project is a level ground project. On the 16th of this month, the current suddenly shifted to the gate of the project, and the old beach collapsed almost completely. The levee foundation collapsed by more than ten zhang. The levee encircling the gate has collapsed, and the gate has also collapsed in two places. There are no materials locally, and the situation is extremely dangerous. Although more than 140 willows have been planted to reduce the scouring force, the levee is still collapsing as of the evening of the 17th. An urgent telegram was sent to the Shangbei Branch to transport the 4,000 sacks of hemp and the 200 cubic meters of new stones currently in the Wenwu flood area to the Xiqin construction site overnight for use. The current was still extremely dangerous on the morning of the 18th. More than ten willows were added to stabilize it slightly. Fearing that the stone boats would go upstream too slowly, an order was issued to purchase 20,000 bricks nearby, load them into bags, and throw them for protection instead of stone. (3) In the Hongqiao project, the current is approaching the levee, and the old beach above the old levee is collapsing rapidly. Only about one zhang of the old beach is left under the levee, and the situation is extremely dangerous. An order was issued to quickly purchase materials to protect it. (4) There is erosion in the levee section of the Baishui County Village and Yangzhuang projects. They are being reinforced separately. (20th)

Rural Relief Plan in Guangdong Province 85

- Program Prepared by the Political Research Association -

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong provincial authorities held a special tariff on the import of foreign rice at the end of last year. The original purpose was to curb the dumping of foreign rice, maintain rural production, and at the same time use this to obtain a sum of money to subsidize rural construction. Since the implementation of this special tariff, the monthly income has been more than one million yuan, which has greatly benefited the provincial treasury. Chen Jitang, Chairman of the Guangdong Political Research Association, proposed to the association that the Guangdong Provincial Government should allocate 5 million yuan from the income of the foreign rice tax to carry out rural relief undertakings in order to comply with government regulations. The association forwarded the proposal to Feng Rui, Director of the Agriculture and Forestry Bureau, to prepare a concrete plan for review. Feng, upon receiving the order, has prepared ten urgent plans based on the current situation of rural villages in the province, along with a budget, and submitted them to the association. The contents of the plan are summarized as follows: (A) Principles (1) To relieve the current urgent needs of farmers, so that the majority of farmers can obtain universal benefits, so as to increase the economic strength of rural villages and the country. (2) The relief work should be based on promoting the modernization of agricultural production, increasing the productivity of individuals and the productivity of land, and improving the quality of products. (3) The funds used for rural relief can be gradually returned from the relief undertakings and then used to develop other economic undertakings in rural villages. (B) Measures (1) Construction of urgently needed farmland water conservancy in various places. (2) Prevention and control of cattle plague throughout the province. (3) Establishment of various important agricultural management areas suitable for local conditions. (4) Development of tropical economic forestry. (5) Undertaking camphor management. (6) Establishment of a Huashui Mountain forest management field. (7) Construction of the Dongjiang River source forest. (8) Increasing rice production. (9) Breeding excellent livestock breeds. (10) Completing the farmer lending organization. (C) Budget, summarizing the above ten items, the temporary start-up cost is 4,068,264 yuan, and the annual recurring cost is 931,736 yuan. The total of temporary and recurring costs is 5,000,000 yuan. (Correspondent of this newspaper, Gan Fangxian)

Songjiang - Improving the Deed Tax Transfer Method 86

The county government received instructions from the Department of Finance yesterday, pointing out the points that should be improved regarding the deed tax and the promotion of transfers, stating briefly that, according to the report of the investigators, the two best points for handling deed tax collection in Jiangyin County (1) The review procedures for promoting transfer should be handled as soon as possible. The official seal form can be obtained on the same day, which reduces the trouble for the villagers and is considered convenient. (2) On the mortgage deed, a wooden chop is added to separately list the regular tax, surtax, official seal form fee, etc., which is convenient for not only the staff to calculate but also for the deed owner to check and avoid the drawbacks of floating collection. After receiving the order, County Chief Jin instructed the donation collection office to comply.

Petition to Jin Province for Corruption in Grain Transportation 87

The case of Ye Zongcheng, the former director of the first national tax collection in this county, who was involved in corruption in grain transportation, has caused a great uproar in the city. It is learned that the Charity Board of the seven counties and other united groups have sent representatives to Jin Province to petition in the hope of achieving a thorough investigation. Suzhou - Criminals in Land Cases Escorted to Province for Interrogation 88

The Provincial Security Department sent personnel to Suzhou last month to crack down on the Chen Qiaji large land yard in Chengde Lane. Seven criminals were arrested one after another and detained in the Public Security Bureau Detention Center. They were escorted to the Provincial Security Department yesterday for interrogation. Also, Shen Gaozhen, the former director of the Wuxian County Public Security Bureau, was suddenly arrested and taken to Beijing by personnel sent to Suzhou by the Capital Garrison Headquarters the day before yesterday. It is heard that it is also related to the case. Wuxi - Young Woman Dies from Abortion 89

Dai, the wife of Wang Shican, the owner of the Wang Xiecheng wood shop in Shuyuan Lane in the city, was about thirty years old. She was romantic and had an affair with a neighbor, Zhang. Recently, she suddenly became pregnant, so she colluded with her lover and husband to have an abortion. The day before yesterday, she went to the midwife Su Wang in Luosijing near Dongting Town to undergo surgery. Unexpectedly, due to the unsuccessful operation, she suddenly experienced severe abdominal pain and unstoppable bleeding. She died in less than five minutes. Afterwards, the news spread throughout the town. The head of the 554th Tu, upon hearing the news, believed that the case involved human life and planned to report it to the court for an examination. He also had someone watch the midwife and notified her husband, Wang Shican, to return home. However, it is heard that the matter has now been settled through mediation by the midwife and Wang Shican has petitioned the court to waive the examination.

Chao - Water Level Lowers Daily, Crops Wither 90

Since the beginning of autumn, the weather has been dry and there has been no rain, making it increasingly difficult for farmers in the four villages to draw water. On the night of the day before yesterday (25th), there was thunder and lightning, and the situation was tense, as if it was about to rain. As a result, no rain fell, causing great disappointment. In recent days, the water level of Taihu Lake has been lowering daily, leveling with the water level of the Grand Canal. There is even a danger of rivers drying up in various tributaries. In the 3rd district, the villagers in Xinan Township south of Xinan Town, including Zhenqiaobang, Zhangzhushibang, Xutaocijingbang, Xiaolongjing, Dabaillongqiao, Xiaobaillongqiao, and Xucaiheqiao, have built dams at both ends of each river in the Taihu Lake direction and the Grand Canal direction to draw water into the rivers and then pump it into the fields in order to save the drought. In the 5th district, the crops in Qianzhou, Beiqifang, and Fuzhou Village have withered due to the difficulty of drawing water, and all the small boats on the inland rivers have also stopped running. There is a panic about drinking water in the urban area, and the authorities are planning to remedy it.

Private Middle Schools in Jiangsu Province 91

Joint Organization Promotion Association

Private middle schools in Jiangsu Province are scattered across various locations and lack a proper organization. Recently, Soochow University Affiliated High School, Private Yangzhong High School, Zhenhua Girls' High School, and other schools have initiated the establishment of the Jiangsu Province Private Middle School Promotion Association, with the specific aim of fostering relationships, exchanging ideas, and increasing educational efficiency. Yesterday at 9:00 AM, a founding conference was held at Private Wuxi High School. Dozens of representatives from middle schools along the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway line and from northern Jiangsu attended. The association's charter was passed on the spot, and nine executive committee members and five supervisory committee members were elected. In the afternoon, executive and supervisory committee meetings continued, with the executive committee mutually electing Wuxi High School, Yangzhong High School, and Soochow University Affiliated High School as standing members. In addition, several important matters were resolved.

Changzhou: New County Magistrate Arrives to Take Office 92

Cai Pei, the county magistrate of Wuyi County, resigned. The provincial government appointed Hou Houzong to succeed him. After being appointed, Hou sent Xie Lvlü to Changzhou once to investigate and to negotiate the handover with the county government. Subsequently, Magistrate Hou decided to arrive in Changzhou on the 26th to take office, and appointed Xie Lvlü as the chief of the First Section, Lü Zezhi as the chief of the Second Section, and requested Shi Ziquan, the former chief, to continue as the chief of the Third Section. Secretary Yang Shucheng is still in Hunan and will arrive in Changzhou within a few days. The chiefs of the First and Second Sections arrived on the evening of the 25th, while Magistrate Hou arrived in Changzhou by train from Zhenjiang at noon today (the 26th).

Villagers Celebrate Rainfall 93

Wuyi has suffered from severe drought this year, with little rainfall. Since autumn, there has been no rain at all, causing extreme anxiety among the villagers and creating social unrest. Yesterday (the 25th) at 4:00 PM, dark clouds gathered and a sudden rainstorm occurred, lasting for about twenty minutes before stopping. Although it did not solve the problem, it did provide some consolation. Also, near the train station, the kiln owners He Niangeng and his brother Niansheng were both struck by lightning at the time. After rescue efforts, Niangeng was fortunate enough to regain consciousness, but Niansheng could not be revived.

Haimen: Madman Commits Arson and Self-Immolation 94

In Zhongnan Township, the first district of Qidong, a farmer named Zhang Guorong suffered from mental illness for many years, with alternating episodes of illness and recovery. The day before yesterday afternoon, the family was working in the fields when Zhang's illness suddenly recurred. He locked the doors and used kerosene to set the house on fire. Thick smoke quickly filled the air, and flames soared. By the time the neighbors noticed, it was too late to help. The three thatched houses where he lived, as well as his belongings, were completely burned down, and Zhang died in the fire, his skin charred and flesh rotten, a truly tragic sight.

Case of Judicial Personnel Embezzlement 95

Dai Chengzhang and Zhang Guirong, clerks of the county government's judicial section, and bailiff Jin Zhigao, repeatedly colluded to accept bribes, alter confessions, and secretly replace important stolen evidence in a theft case involving a Zhang surname. The day before yesterday (the 23rd), Judge Xu discovered this and was greatly angered. He immediately placed Dai, Zhang, and Jin under guard and held a court hearing that evening. Due to the seriousness of the case, onlookers were prohibited. As a result, Zhang Guirong and Jin Zhigao were detained, while Dai Chengzhang was released on bail.

Jiaxing: Villagers in Xincheng Township Loot Rice 96

Shen Zhenxing, Hengchang, Gongmaoxing, and other rice shops in the South Village of Xincheng Town, Jiaxing, used boats on the afternoon of the 25th to transport large quantities of rice for sale elsewhere. When the boats were transported to the countryside, hungry villagers spotted them and gathered to loot the rice. When the Xincheng Town police heard the news, they went to suppress the looting. The hungry villagers refused to listen to their warnings, so the police fired warning shots, causing a farmer to fall to the ground after being hit by a bullet. The police then returned to the town. The villagers, because someone had been injured, swarmed to the town in the hundreds. They were dispersed after local figures persuaded them. It is now known that Shen Zhenxing had more than ninety dan of rice looted, while Hengchang and Gongmaoxing each had thirty to forty dan looted.

Shaoxing: Major Fire at Dayun Bridge in the City 97

A fire suddenly broke out at Dayun Bridge in the city at 1:00 PM on the 25th. The fire started at Feng Tongxing's tofu shop and quickly spread to more than thirty households on both sides, including Heshengtang Store, Xianheng Branch Garden, Dazhang Salt Shop, Yuekang Southern Goods Store, Xie Yuanxing Rice Cake Shop, Cutaixing Southern Goods Store, Renhe Meat Shop, and the gatehouses of the Mo and Ren families, housing more than twenty families. It took three hours to extinguish the fire, which destroyed more than one hundred houses, making it the largest fire in recent memory.

Xiaoshan: Two Villages Fight Over Water 98

Sun Yuangui and other farmers in Xiaoshan's Fourth District, Xiaohu Sun area, built a dam to draw water to irrigate their fields. The Xu family in the neighboring village objected, claiming it affected their drinking water, leading to a fight between the two families. On the 20th, more than a thousand people from the two villages gathered, firing blunderbusses and cannons at random, intending to level each other's villages. Women and children fled in terror, as if facing a major enemy. Fortunately, the Linpu Public Security Bureau learned of the incident and went to suppress it, bringing the situation under control.

Guangde: Severe Drought in Guangde, Southern Anhui 99

Guangde is located on the edge of southern Anhui, bordering Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The county's main products are grain and rice, along with bamboo, timber, charcoal, and Sanliu writing paper. The entire area is surrounded by mountains and not far from the sea, so it has never experienced major droughts or floods. Since the Red Bandits ravaged the area in 1929, the rural economy has collapsed. The average annual harvest is only 60% of what it used to be, and the farmers' suffering is indescribable. Fortunately, in recent years, the rainfall during the planting season has been relatively good, so there has been no need to draw water for transplanting rice, and the fields have not been abandoned. This year, the rainfall was also adequate in late spring and early summer, but since the seventh day of the fourth month of the lunar calendar, more than one hundred days have passed without rain. The drought is severe, bamboo and trees have withered, the ground is scorched yellow, and livestock lack pasture. A few areas have received one or two light rains, but they have been insufficient. The damage to paddy fields can be divided into three categories: (1) About 10% of the fields could not be planted because there was no water to draw at the time of transplanting. (2) About 20% of the fields were irrigated but will only yield 10-20% of the harvest if sufficient rain falls within days. (3) The remaining 70% will have no harvest at all. As for dry land, soybeans and other grains were planted three times but failed to germinate. Under the current economic conditions, farming families resort to pawning and borrowing whenever it is time to plant, hoping to make a small income to make ends meet. This disaster has left them completely hopeless. Now, the healthy ones are taking their families to beg for food elsewhere, and suicides among the elderly and weak are heard of daily. Cunning individuals are robbing and looting food, or stealing unripe dry rice under cover of darkness. People are panicking to the extreme. According to the elderly, such a severe drought has not been seen since 1856, more than eighty years ago.

Jinan: Cai Renbao Guides Silkworm Rearing in Shandong 100

The National Economic Commission's Silk Improvement Committee, seeking to revive the silk industry in Shandong Province, sent Commissioner He Shangping and Technical Specialist Wang Jiayou from Shanghai via Qingdao last month to visit Mayor Shen and then travel to Jinan to meet with Shandong Chairman Han Fuqu and Construction Department Director Zhang Honglie to discuss relief measures. Chairman Han and Director Zhang both agreed that the silk industry urgently needed relief. He and Wang learned in detail about the silk industry situation in Shandong from repeatedly reports by silk expert Cai Renbao. Furthermore, Cai is the son of silk magnate Cai Cimu and has rich experience in the silk industry. Cai was still in Shandong, so they visited him and discussed the matter in detail. They decided to invite Cai to assist in inspecting various places. At the beginning of the month, Cai returned south for personal matters and met with Standing Committee members Zeng Yangfu and He Shangping to discuss new silkworm rearing test methods. It was decided to send personnel to Shandong to bring seeds and provide guidance, and the committee sent a letter to the Shandong Construction Department in advance to make arrangements. It is now learned that Lv Yicheng and Xia Chubai, the technicians sent by the committee to guide the new silkworm rearing, departed from the Zhejiang Silk Improvement Association with the new silkworm seeds the day before yesterday and arrived in Jinan. In the morning, they visited Director Zhang Honglie and First Section Chief Zhu Guixun of the Construction Department to make arrangements. It was decided that they would go to Linqu yesterday to guide the trial rearing. The equipment and assistants will be provided by Dai Guanxun, director of the Yidu Sericulture Experiment Station, and Chen Shican, a technician from the Construction Department, will be responsible for distributing the silkworm seeds. The fresh cocoons produced in the future will be purchased at high prices to encourage the industry. Lv and Xia visited Cai's residence, accompanied by Mr. Zhao Songbi and Xu Baohua, because Lv and Xia were instructed by the standing committee members Zeng, He, Ge, and Zhang to consult with Cai on methods at any time. After the talks, Cai fell ill due to fatigue from traveling, so Zhao Songbi and Xu Baohua accompanied them to visit the scenic Daming Lake and hosted a banquet to welcome them. In addition to instructing the Yidu Sericulture Experiment Station to cooperate, the Construction Department will also send Technician Chen to Yidu yesterday to proceed to Linqu and begin work.

Today is Confucius's Birthday 101

Various Circles Hold Commemorative Assembly

At 10:00 AM in the Dacheng Hall of the Civic Education Center

Wu Tiecheng, Tong Xingbai, etc. Appointed as Chairmen

All Schools, Institutions, and Factories are Closed

Today is the birthday of the great teacher Confucius. According to the commemorative methods promulgated by the central government, all sectors of the city's party, government, business, academia, labor, and agriculture will hold a commemorative assembly at 10:00 AM this morning in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road to honor his sacred virtues. All schools, institutions, factories, etc. in the city will be closed for one day. Details are recorded as follows:

(Assembly Venue Arrangement) The commemorative assembly venue is located in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal Public Education Center. In the center of the hall hangs a portrait of the Premier and the Party and National Flags, below which hangs a portrait of Confucius specially painted by the municipal government. On both sides are arranged the bells, drums, qin, and se of the Datong Musical Society, musical instruments for temple ceremonies. A temporary shed has been built outside the hall to serve as the guest seating area. The various sacrificial vessels originally displayed have been moved to the lecture hall for display and viewing.

(Assembly Officials) The presidium of the commemorative assembly is set at seven people, including Tong Xingbai of the Municipal Party Department, Wu Tiecheng of the Municipal Government, Yang Hu of the Municipal Security Department, Tao Baichuan of the Municipal Education Association, Yu Zuoting of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhu Xuefan of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, and Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Agricultural Association. The recorder is Tong Muge, the master of ceremonies is Zhang Hanyun, and the reception and security are handled by officials from the Municipal Government and the Municipal Party Department. The Municipal Public Security Bureau is requested to send police to maintain order.

(Assembly Order) The order of the assembly is determined as follows: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Music (Public Security Bureau Military Band, Datong Musical Society); (3) Sing the Party Song; (4) Bow three times to the Party and National Flags, the Premier's portrait, and the Confucius portrait; (5) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's testament; (6) The chairman reports the significance of commemorating Confucius; (7) Speeches; (8) Music; (9) Ceremony concludes.

(One-Day Holiday) All major and minor schools and various institutions and factories in the city, in addition to sending one representative with a letter to participate in the commemorative assembly, will also hold separate commemorative ceremonies at their respective schools, reporting on Confucius's actions of practicing what he preached and loving learning, to show respect. The Municipal Education Bureau has already notified all major and minor schools yesterday and instructed them on how to arrange the auditorium.

(Zhonghe Shaole) The local Datong Musical Society originally intended to perform Zhonghe Shaole sacrifice music for Confucius on Confucius's birthday at the World Society. However, because the rituals promulgated by the National Government do not include sacrifices, the method has been changed. Today, all members will gather, bring their instruments, and participate in the commemorative assembly to play Zhonghe Shaole music, expressing their respect.

Belgian Royal Envoy 102

Johnson Arrives in Shanghai This Morning

Scheduled to Meet Chairman Lin on the Eighth

Baron Johnson, the special envoy sent by the new Belgian King to the Far East, along with his wife and a group of eight people, arrived in Java last month for sightseeing. They are now arriving in China on the French postal ship Aramis. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai this morning. The details are as follows:

(Arrives This Morning) According to the French Postal Company, the ship is scheduled to enter the port around 4:00 AM and is expected to arrive at the port around 6:00 AM, docking at the China Merchants Northern Wharf in Yangshupu. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has telegraphed its Shanghai office to send Section Chief Zhao Tiezhang as a representative to welcome them, along with Mr. Jiyoumu representing the Belgian legation, acting as Consul General Tan Erfu. In addition, those preparing to welcome them at the pier include Tang Shixuan, the Shanghai Municipal Government representative, and representatives of the Belgian community. The Belgian Consulate has booked rooms at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund to accommodate Johnson and his party.

(Traveling Companions) In addition to his wife and son, Johnson is accompanied by eight people, including the royal family, Mr. and Mrs. Ya Tuo, Mr. Hailmen, Mr. Gaikehefu, and Mr. Meng Yunlong. Johnson is a prominent figure in Belgian financial and business circles, managing many large-scale banks and companies, and wielding considerable influence in various industries. He also holds a significant position in politics.

(Itinerary in China) Johnson's itinerary in China is scheduled as follows: After arriving in Shanghai this morning, he will attend a public banquet hosted by the Belgian Consulate and the Belgian business community at noon. Tomorrow afternoon at 4:00 PM, he will take the Shanghai-Ping Railway north to Xuzhou, and then travel from Xuzhou along the Longhai Railway to visit Kaifeng and Luoyang on the 29th or 30th. He will arrive in Peiping on the 31st and stay for five days of sightseeing. On the afternoon of the 5th of next month, he will travel south accompanied by Mr. and Mrs. Jiyoumu of the Belgian Legation. He will stay in Tianjin for one day. On the afternoon of the 6th, he will leave Tianjin and arrive in Nanjing on the evening of the 7th. On the morning of the 8th, he will meet with Chairman Lin at 10:00 AM. In the evening, he will be hosted by President Wang. On the evening of the 9th, he will take the night express train at 11:00 PM from Nanjing back to Shanghai.

(Scheduled Departure to Japan) After returning to Shanghai, he will attend a banquet hosted by Mayor Wu Tiecheng on the evening of the 10th. After resting briefly in Shanghai, he will depart from Shanghai on the Italian postal ship Conte Verde on the morning of the 11th to visit Japan and return thanks for the visit from the Japanese government.

City Temperature 103

Slightly Lower Than Yesterday

Hope for an Early and Abundant Rain

Since the beginning of autumn in the city, the daily temperature has generally been around 100 degrees. On the 24th, it rose to 100 degrees, and on the 25th, it suddenly rose to 104 degrees, the highest autumn temperature recorded by the Observatory in 63 years. Although it was sunny and hot yesterday, the north wind brought relief, so the highest temperature dropped to 99.5 degrees, which seemed slightly cooler than the previous two days. However, the drought has been prolonged, and there is no sign of rain. Drinking water sources in various places are drying up, farmland is cracking, epidemics are spreading, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. It is hoped that Heaven will have pity on the common people and send abundant rain soon, which may still provide a glimmer of hope for salvation.

Shanghai Fishing Industry Plans to Establish 104

National Marine Products Company

Preparatory Office Located on Limalu Road in the Sixteenth Concession

Shanghai fishing industry magnates Zhou Wangyue, Jin Chuxiang, and others, recognizing the decline of China's fishing industry and the opportunistic encroachment by the Japanese, with annual imports of marine products reaching a staggering 40 million yuan, are planning to raise 500,000 yuan in Shanghai to establish a large-scale marine products company to develop the fishing industry and recover lost rights. The preparations are currently underway, and the company is expected to be formally established within the year. A reporter from China Eastern News Agency visited the company's preparatory office on Limalu Road in the Sixteenth Concession yesterday to learn the details, which are recorded as follows:

(500,000 Yuan to Establish Company) The company will be named "National Marine Products Co., Ltd.," with a capital of 500,000 yuan. It has already obtained the support of the majority of the Shanghai fishing industry and has submitted an application to the Ministry of Industry for record. After reviewing the application, the Ministry of Industry found that it was in line with the salt-fishing manufacturing plant planned in the Ministry's four-year fishing industry plan and approved its promotion. Preparations are now underway to formally establish the company and begin operations within this year.

(Scope of Business) The company's scope of business is roughly divided into the following four items: (1) Establishing marine product manufacturing plants in four important fishing areas along the coasts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang: Shengshan, Sijiao, Daishan, and Zhoushan, to enable cooperation between fishermen; (2) Owning gasoline transport ships to collect catches from fishing boats and transport fresh goods; (3) Establishing a natural ice factory and warehouses; (4) Organizing fishing cooperative societies, etc. In the future, the company plans to purchase fishing vessels to engage in fishing and shellfish farming to increase production, depending on the development of the business. The total annual turnover is expected to be over 10 million yuan.

(Surveying the Annual Yield of Fishing Grounds) The company believes that in order to develop this industry, it must first understand the fishing situation. It has conducted extensive surveys in various coastal fishing areas, including Xiangshan, Zhenhai, Taizhou, Wenzhou, Shengshan, Sijiao, and Daishan. According to statistics, the annual output is approximately 1.6 million dan of yellow croaker, over 570,000 dan of large yellow croaker, approximately 300,000 dan of black seabream, over 360,000 dan of ribbonfish, and approximately 200,000 dan of jellyfish skin. Other fish such as shark, pomfret, reeves shad, mussels, whitebait, and seaweed also have detailed statistics.

(Improving the Plan, First Establish Manufacturing Plants) In order to improve the fishing industry easily and meet needs, the company decided to start with the establishment of marine product manufacturing plants. It has hired specialized personnel to conduct research. Within the manufacturing plants, there are separate departments for salting fish, drying fish, and canning fish. All products are refined using scientific methods to ensure that they last a long time and are properly seasoned. A fishing boat affairs agency is also attached to supply fishermen with various needs, so that fishermen can reduce the burden, focus on fishing, and promote the benefits of marine products.

Report from Shanghai Municipal Council's Rates Office 105

Index of Vacant Houses Increases

Mr. MacFee, acting director of the Finance Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, and Mr. Bourne, deputy director and head of the tax division, released the summer housing tax statistics for this year, which amounted to 2,638,866 yuan, an increase of 210,092 yuan compared to the same period last year. However, one notable statistic is the increasing number of vacant houses. In the summer of 1932, there were 1,292 Western-style vacant houses and 3,395 Chinese-style vacant houses in the International Settlement. By the summer of last year (1933), this had increased to 1,453 Western-style vacant houses and 4,153 Chinese-style vacant houses. This summer, the number of vacant houses has further increased to 1,859 Western-style vacant houses and 4,424 Chinese-style vacant houses. The vacant houses in the northern and southern districts and the French Concession are not included. The economic downturn is evident.

Russian Ship Flees to Wusong Port 106

Although They Have Passports, They Are Not Signed

The Ship is Under the Guard of the Public Security Bureau

According to the Shanghai Times, nine Russians, including one woman, reportedly fled from Vladivostok in a motor tugboat. They encountered a storm north of Jeju Island and were in danger, but were rescued by the islanders on August 16. They claimed to have fled to Shanghai because of the oppression of the Vladivostok police authorities. The captain, Mr. Pisorov, claimed to be an American citizen, and the woman on board was said to be his wife. After repairing the engine, they continued to Shanghai, arriving at noon on Saturday (the 25th), thirteen days after fleeing Vladivostok. When the ship arrived at Wusong Port, it was thoroughly searched by the water police. Two pistols, one rifle, and one giant sword were reportedly found. Although the people carried Soviet passports, they were not signed by the appropriate officials and they did not have ship manifests. The people have requested permission to reside in Shanghai, and this matter will be decided by the Shanghai Municipal Government. The ship is currently under the guard of the Wusong Port Public Security Bureau, and the people remain on board. It is expected that the local Soviet authorities will lodge a protest and request that the people be detained and that the ship be seized as Soviet property.

Lake Society Concerned About Drought in Hometown 110

Telegrams to Zhejiang Provincial Government Requesting Investigation of Disaster in Huzhou - Guizhou Road

The Lake Society has received successive reports from hometowns in the six counties of Huzhou, stating that the disaster situation is extremely serious and that the people are scattered and displaced, a truly tragic sight. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to the Zhejiang Provincial Government requesting that personnel be dispatched to investigate the actual disaster situation, distinguish between the severity of the situation, reduce or exempt land taxes, and postpone the collection of old debts. In addition, rivers and canals should be dredged to provide work relief. The original telegram is as follows: "To Chairman Lu of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, this summer has been severely dry, and there has been no rain in the autumn. The lakes and ponds have dried up, the fields have cracked, the crops have withered, and the harvest is disappointing. Successive reports have been received from hometowns in the six counties of the old Huzhou region, stating that the disaster situation is extremely serious. It is sincerely requested that personnel be dispatched quickly to investigate the actual disaster situation, distinguish between the severity of the situation, reduce or exempt land taxes, and postpone the collection of old debts. In addition, rivers and canals should be dredged to provide work relief, and measures should be taken to provide relief, hoping to alleviate the suffering. The telegram is sent with the utmost urgency. Respectfully, Chen Qicai, Chairman of the Lake Society."

Telegram to Wuxing County Magistrate Requesting Relief for People's Drinking Water. Because the river channels have dried up, the drinking water is polluted, and diseases are spreading, the Lake Society sent a telegram to the Wuxing County Magistrate, urging him to hire more civilian boats and laborers to transport water from places such as Yixi Bridge outside the South Gate of Huzhou, Datong Bridge outside the North Gate, and Longxikou outside the West Gate to the city to provide drinking water for the people. Each load may charge the lowest shipping fee to subsidize and emphasize public health.

County Government Notice 111

Land and Property Transfer Collection

The Shanghai County Government is now notifying that there are unavoidable cases where the previous owners of real estate purchased or mortgaged in this county have failed to collect the transfer, or have already collected the transfer and have not received the official seal. To protect the property rights of each household and squeeze out the deed tax, supplementary measures have been drafted. All households that have failed to collect the transfer or have already collected the transfer but have not received the official seal and deed paper after the establishment of the transfer collection office in September 1932, are allowed to submit the deed to the county within three months to pay the tax. After the county verifies that the records match, a supplementary official seal will be issued to provide protection. In addition to ordering the transfer collection office to comply, all property owners are hereby notified.

American Loaned Cotton 112

120,000 Bales Not Sold

Whether Chinese Cotton Mills Purchase It or Not

Decision Depends on the Price of New Cotton

After the National Government obtained a loan of 20 million yuan in American cotton and wheat flour from the United States, the cotton and wheat flour have been packed by Fulyen & Co. and continuously transported to Shanghai. All of the wheat flour has been purchased by domestic flour manufacturers. This year's drought has resulted in poor harvests of agricultural products in various places, causing food shortages. Therefore, flour prices are also soaring. Before February, the selling price was 1.9 yuan per bag, but now it must be sold for 2.65 yuan. The flour manufacturers who purchased the American wheat flour are all making huge profits. Although more than 100,000 bales of American cotton have been sold by Fulyen & Co. to foreign merchants, there are currently 120,000 bales remaining unsold. The government plans to sell them to Chinese spinning mills, but the mills are considering whether the price of new cotton is cost effective, because this year's cotton production in China, according to the Cotton Statistics Association's survey and forecast, is more abundant than in previous years. The seeds for the American cotton grown in Shaanxi and Jiangsu are long and thick. The new cotton from Tongzhou, Jiangsu, has already entered the market, and other provinces will also produce cotton in mid-September. Although American cotton can be spun into fine yarn, if the price is too high compared to the price of domestic cotton, it will be difficult for cotton mills to purchase American cotton.

Preliminary Agreement Reached

The World News Agency reports that the Zhejiang Provincial Government, facing severe drought and crop failure this year, urgently needs to provide relief to farmers. Due to insufficient funds in the provincial treasury, the provincial government decided to issue 20 million yuan in local public bonds. Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Reconstruction, traveled to Shanghai and then to Nanjing to present the severity of the disaster to the Central Government, arguing that issuing public bonds was the only way to ensure proper post-disaster recovery and urging for Central Government approval. The issuance of these bonds has now been approved by the Executive Yuan, pending subsequent ratification by the Legislative Yuan. Zeng emphasizes the severity of the disaster in Zhejiang Province and the urgent need to complete a portion of highway construction. Therefore, the mortgage of these public bonds needs to be negotiated as soon as possible to remit funds to Zhejiang for use. Consequently, further discussions with leading figures in the banking community are scheduled for today to determine the specific arrangements.
