Page 17

Shen Bao Medical Weekly

Strategies for Medical Development (Continued) 199

— Song Guobin

(Decimos) Unite All Factions for a Grand Unity. The discussion of medical factions has been confusing for some time. All of us in the profession are aware of it. The idea of unity has been mentioned repeatedly. However, the reason why it has not yet been realized is that the opinions of various factions have not been fully aligned. It is not necessary for everyone to be of one mind, but if we concentrate our strength, it will be easier to achieve success. Otherwise, there will be discord, with some dominating and others being subservient. Opinions will fill the room, but no consensus will be reached. The implementation of any matter will inevitably face opposition from different factions, which will hinder progress from all sides. Therefore, if the medical community wants to have a massive force and the development of new medicine, it is essential to integrate all factions and achieve a grand unity.

(Zi) Eliminate Undesirable Elements. In any organization, there will inevitably be a mixture of good and bad elements. The good ones will devote their minds and efforts to seeking the happiness of the organization. The undesirable ones, however, will use their jealousy and harmful abilities to pursue their ambitions of vying for power and profit. If they are not satisfied, they will not hesitate to resort to disruptive measures to engage in sabotage. Therefore, if these elements are not removed, it will be difficult for the organization's undertakings to succeed. We must concentrate our efforts on conducting on-site investigations. If we discover any individuals who are plotting conspiracies or falsely using the organization's name to engage in deceitful activities, we must deal with them and expel them. In this way, the internal affairs will be cleared up, and we will not be burdened by harmful elements.

(Chou) Research Methods to Protect the Medical Profession. Doctors should possess the necessary ethics and enjoy the rights and benefits they deserve. However, the so-called medical rights have their own special position and cannot be encompassed by ordinary human rights. Ordinary laws impose heavy penalties for injury, intimidation, and the use of anesthetics and narcotics. However, due to the nature of their work, doctors have no way to avoid the aforementioned items. Therefore, if doctors do these things, they should not be considered as breaking the law. However, while this phenomenon gives doctors a special status, there is no clear provision in the law. As a result, doctors are constantly in a state of violating the law without real protection. In recent years, medical disputes have become increasingly frequent. Doctors are constantly appearing in court for treating patients. If we do not find ways to protect them, then any autopsy, any surgery, any injection, any change of wording can become grounds for accusations. We must urge the government to promulgate a law to protect doctors as soon as possible. At the same time, we must, from the organization's perspective, refer to the established rules of Western countries and combine them with our country's customs and traditions to conduct thorough research on methods to protect the medical profession, so as to provide a reference for the government. In this way, the medical profession will have a defense and will not be subject to innocent infringements at any time.

(Yin) Limit the Production of Unofficial Doctors. As worms live in wood and destroy the wood, so do quack doctors destroy medicine. This is why we have been sternly refuting unofficial doctors for many years. When we examine the reasons for their emergence, we find that some are nurses from hospitals, some are apprentices of private individuals, some are from correspondence medical schools, and some are from medical schools with incomplete facilities. All of these are sources of unofficial doctors, and the responsibility for them should be borne by official doctors. If we want to promote a career, we must first engage in internal rectification. If we want to eliminate a disease, we must first cut off its roots. If we can use the strength of the organization to provide appropriate training for existing unofficial doctors and prevent the continued emergence of future unofficial doctors, then after the old ones gradually decrease, China's medical community will naturally return to purity.

In summary, the above thirteen items, although they are clichés, are actually necessary strategies for medical proposals. Although medicine is a small path, it is of utmost importance to the revival of the nation. Only with a healthy people can we talk about ways to strengthen the country and the race and ways to wipe out humiliation and resist insults. The responsibility borne by the medical community is not insignificant. Therefore, medical development, on a small scale, is to seek independence and development for the medical community; on a large scale, it is to seek health and revival for the entire nation. Otherwise, why would we expand and enlarge the affairs of one sector to call it development?

Someone asked, "There are thousands of things in the medical community that need to be implemented. You have only mentioned thirteen items. Aren't you missing a lot?" I do not know that these thirteen items can actually encompass everything and are the foundation of medical development. Why do I say this? Education is the source of talent and the foundation of all undertakings. When the foundation is deep, the tree will be lush. When the source is far, the stream will be long. Therefore, we must first focus on medical education. The most important thing in medical education is to establish curriculum standards. With standards, talent can tend to be consistent. The most important thing in standards is to emphasize both academic theory and experience. When both are emphasized, the treatment of diseases can be guaranteed to be safe. However, this is related to academics, and the cultivation of morality is even more important. Therefore, it is necessary to add a course on medical ethics. Unqualified medical schools have been improved and eliminated due to non-compliance with standards. It is even more necessary to add qualified medical schools to prepare for the emergence of official doctors. In this way, all aspects will be taken care of, and the problem of medical education seems to be solvable. As for medical administration, it is of great importance to the interests of medical affairs throughout the country. The most important medical institution in the country is the hospital. Therefore, we must first formulate hospital standards and then use this goal as a target to eliminate those that do not meet the standards and increase those that meet the standards. The greatest enemies of the medical community are the inherent old doctors and the imported foreign doctors. If we restrict them at the same time, then medical administration can avoid divergence, and the rights and interests will not flow out. Then, we can proceed to promulgate laws and regulations to protect new medicine without any obstacles. The above items are all things that the government should do. There are also things that have nothing to do with the government and need to be done by our medical community ourselves, and that is the medical association. Although the medical association has no political background, it has a personal stake in the matter. It is different from those who have nothing to do with it. Since it is called an organization, there can be no phenomenon of factional divisions. Therefore, we must first unite with sincerity. Only after unity can we eliminate undesirable elements and limit the production of unofficial doctors. As for the research on methods to protect the medical profession, it is an important task of the medical association. The medical association is in a position to serve the medical community and has a consulting position for the government. It cannot be ignored simply because it is an organization of one sector.

From this perspective, these thirteen items are actually fundamental strategies and have continuity and correspondence. Over the years, medical colleagues and I have spoken about them repeatedly, but they have not yet been put into practice. Therefore, I have specially reorganized them and listed them item by item for the reference of those who care about the progress of medical affairs.

The first paragraph (Decimos) should be placed before "Medical Organization Aspect" in the previous issue (3). Special correction is made.

P> Common Sense Q&A About Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(3) (10) (7) Chronic Habitual Constipation

(Q) What is called chronic habitual constipation?

(A) Chronic habitual constipation is a disease in which feces are retained in the large intestine for a long time due to functional impairment.

(Q) What are the causes of this disease?

(A) There are many causes of chronic habitual constipation. First, it is eating too much meat, eggs, refined flour, and other foods that lack fiber. Second, it is due to excessive use of enemas. Third, it is due to physical constitution or opium addiction, which reduces the peristaltic function of the intestines. Fourth, it is spasm of the large intestine muscles. Fifth, it is persistent organic diseases of other organs, such as gastric ulcer, duodenal ulcer, cholecystitis, chronic appendicitis, gynecological diseases, prostate disease, hemorrhoids, and anal fissures. Sixth, endocrine disorders, such as pregnancy and hypothyroidism, are also causes.

(Q) Are the symptoms of this chronic habitual constipation the same?

(A) They are not uniform. In some cases, the feces only remain in the cecum, ascending colon, and the right one-third of the transverse colon, while the rest of the large intestine remains empty. In some cases, the passage of feces is very slow. In some cases, spasms occur in the transverse colon, descending colon, and sigmoid colon, causing the intestinal wall to collapse. In some cases, the entire large intestine has no abnormalities, and only the rectum lacks sensation, making it difficult to feel the urge to defecate.

(Q) What are the symptoms of chronic habitual constipation?

(A) Bowel movements are very slow, feces form hard lumps, there is a feeling of bloating in the abdomen, a heavy feeling in the head, congestion in the head, general fatigue, aversion to work, insomnia, and loss of appetite.

(Q) Can habitual constipation be corrected by changing habits?

(A) Yes. Patients should go to the toilet at a fixed time every day to develop a habit. Over time, they can be on time.

Page 18

for bowel movements.

(Q) Can this disease be treated with diet therapy?

(A) Diet therapy is effective in children, but less effective in the elderly. It is even less effective in those who use strong laxatives frequently.

(Q) What foods have a laxative effect?

(A) There are many kinds of such foods, but they are only effective for constipation caused by intestinal muscle relaxation. Such as sugars (honey, sweet fruits, candies, etc.), organic acids (citric acid, sour fruits), salts, mineral water, soda water, fats, cod liver oil, olive oil, plant fiber (vegetables, soybeans, etc.), and cold drinks.

(Q) What medicines can be used to effectively treat habitual constipation?

(A) In drug treatment, it is necessary to first determine whether the constipation is spastic or atonic. Only after determining this can a prescription be given.

(Q) What medicine should be used for spastic habitual constipation?

(A) For spastic constipation, bromine preparations, hyoscyamus preparations, atropine, papaverine, etc. should be used.

(Q) What medicine should be used for atonic habitual constipation?

(A) For atonic constipation, laxatives can be taken, but it is best not to use them. Some laxatives are temporary, such as castor oil, senna leaf infusion, and magnesium sulfate. Those that can be used permanently include lactose, olive oil, liquid paraffin, rhubarb powder, calcined magnesium, peroxidized magnesium, and cascara extract.

(Q) What method should be used to treat cases where it is difficult to feel the urge to defecate due to a lack of sensation in the rectum alone?

(A) An enema can be performed at this time. The method is to use 5 to 20 cubic centimeters of glycerin, diluted with twice the amount of water, and inject it into the anus. Alternatively, soapy water (2-3%), pure water, salt water, olive oil, sesame oil, etc. can be used for the enema. (The end)

Casual Remarks on Vaccination 200

— Zang Hebai

Vaccination is a very common, very old, and very democratic matter, without any class system. I remember that Mr. Cheng Hanzhang and others have already published its theory and operation methods, so there is no need for me to turn on the record player and repeat it again. Now I will talk about the general public's misunderstanding of the original intention of vaccination and the various matters that occur during vaccination!

Our purpose of vaccination is to prevent the spread of smallpox. In other words, it is because smallpox is a disease that, once infected, there is no particularly effective medicine to cure it. If the nursing care is improper and the process is not good, it will be fatal and very dangerous! After vaccination, one will not be infected with this terrible disease within a certain period of time! It does not mean that after vaccination, all sores, boils, ringworm, ulcers, eczema, and rot, as well as symptoms that occur in internal medicine diseases, such as edema, sallow complexion, and loss of appetite, will not occur! If one does not develop sores, boils, ringworm, ulcers, eczema, and rot, as well as symptoms that occur in internal medicine diseases, such as edema, sallow complexion, and loss of appetite, after vaccination; then it should not be called vaccination, but should be called sore planting, boil planting, etc. The name itself is fundamentally wrong! Therefore, it is wrong to expect vaccination to prevent diseases other than smallpox.

The old method of vaccination is already outdated; because its serum and its technique do not conform to the principles of disinfection, there is a risk of spreading other diseases. Except for the general ignorant people who are still practicing the old tricks in remote areas, it should no longer exist in large cities. However, the fact tells us that the words "Mr. So-and-so has received cowpox vaccination by the Chinese method and is transmitting the serum on a certain day" are still often sent to our eyes. In the lower and middle classes, being bewitched by him and becoming his patron can be said to be a lack of common knowledge, which is not to be blamed! What is most incredible is that some people who have received scientific training also become his patrons, reversing the course without knowing it, which is truly contradictory!

In the mouths of these old-fashioned cowpox vaccination doctors, they say, "The old-fashioned cowpox vaccination is thorough, and you don't need to be vaccinated twice in your life," but when we revaccinate people, we encounter many, many people who have been vaccinated with the old-fashioned cowpox and still develop the disease. My wife and my nephew are good examples. They were all vaccinated with the old-fashioned cowpox thirty or twenty years ago. In the past ten years, I have vaccinated them, and they have all developed the disease twice. Where is the "thorough"? Furthermore, when we see patients with smallpox, it is true that many cases occur because their guardians neglected to vaccinate their children in time. However, there are also many, many cases of people in their decades of age who develop smallpox. Did they not receive the old-fashioned cowpox vaccination decades ago? Where is the saying "you don't need to be vaccinated twice in your life"?

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (18) 201

— Hu Jiayan

Chapter 7 General Symptoms of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

Speaking of the symptoms of pulmonary tuberculosis, it fits well with an old Chinese saying: a complete twenty-four history, I really don't know where to start. It is a matter of thousands of threads. I dare to say boldly that almost all disease symptoms can be directly or indirectly attributed to pulmonary tuberculosis. Its course is mostly chronic; in the beginning, it is mostly latent, and there are few obvious symptoms that can be guessed at a glance. Sometimes the patient coughs and feels difficulty in expectorating phlegm, which is the same as ordinary "tracheobronchitis"; many patients feel that this is a bit of a cold, and of course they will not pay special attention to it. Sometimes there are no other symptoms except for poor appetite, and everyone treats this as "gastritis." Some women have a pale complexion and irregular menstruation. These few symptoms easily lead people to imagine "chlorosis." Sometimes there is insomnia, fatigue, and poor appetite, which are very similar to ordinary "neurasthenia." These are all common and habitual, but this point alone has made patients confused; even the correct understanding of doctors is also very difficult. In addition, we know that the beginning of pulmonary tuberculosis is mostly inseparable from the hilar lymph nodes; this aspect is of course close to the nerves. If the vagus nerve (the tenth cranial nerve) is compressed by the swollen gland, then the patient will experience palpitations and severe stomach pain, and it is also difficult to imagine that these symptoms are related to the lungs. Night sweats are comparatively considered to be an obvious symptom of the beginning of the disease, but it is sometimes present in neurasthenia. Based on these facts, we can know that the initial condition of this disease is all-encompassing; a firm diagnosis of right and wrong is certainly not possible for a while; even the determination of the initial date of onset, I am afraid that no one can completely answer.

If the above-mentioned symptoms are indeed pulmonary tuberculosis, then of course they will not stop for no reason; they will flourish from then on. As time goes by, the patient gradually becomes thinner and lighter; if the patient has a little common sense, they will know that they should measure their body temperature. If the result is indeed increasing, and it is very average every day; they also know that this phenomenon is definitely not without cause, and of course they must seek a doctor to examine it in detail. However, most patients still do not pay much attention; and the symptom of elevated body temperature is not felt by the patient himself except when measured with a thermometer. It was not until the symptoms of coughing and sputum in the lungs themselves became more and more obvious, the weight loss was even greater, or blood streaks were found in the sputum, that this cough with blood symptoms was almost like a final warning to the patient. At this time, the patients also know that they can no longer be careless; but the root of tuberculosis has already reached a considerable degree, and it can be asserted that the treatment is not as easy as it was at the beginning.

Common Sense on Ear, Nose, Throat and Eye Hygiene 202

— Tang Renjin

(12) Lacunar Tonsillitis

The hypertrophy and proliferation of the tonsils have already been discussed in the previous two issues. Now, we will talk about its inflammation. This inflammation has various names in clinical practice due to the differences in its location and pathology. The type of tonsillitis discussed in this article is an acute infectious palatine tonsillitis, which is the most common type of tonsillitis (generally, the term “mammary moth swelling” or “sore throat” in common parlance mostly refers to this disease). This disease occurs most often in adults around the age of twenty to thirty. It is less common in children. There is no gender correlation; it cannot be said that it occurs more in men or less in women. People with tonsillar hypertrophy are more susceptible to this disease. Conversely, it is rare in the elderly whose tonsils have already undergone physiological atrophy. This disease is related to rheumatism (commonly known as rheumatic pain), which is a fact recognized by the medical community recently. Having had tonsillitis once does not mean it will not occur a second time, and it may even occur frequently. This can be called habitual angina (Angina habitualis). This disease is often epidemic, so it is frequently encountered in families, schools, armies, prisons, and other places. Its main infectious pathogen is streptococcus, followed by staphylococcus and pneumococcus. This disease is also related to the climate. For example, it is more likely to occur in humid and cold climates and drastic temperature changes. Therefore, statistically, it is most common in August and September, followed by October, November, December, January, and July. The onset of the disease usually begins with chills and shivering, followed by fever, often reaching around 40 degrees Celsius. At the same time, there is a feeling of pain in the throat, which is even more intense when swallowing. Sleep is restless at night. The pain often spreads to the ears, so patients often hold their ears with their hands, showing a look of distress. Speech and diet become inconvenient. The whole body falls into a state of fatigue. There is headache, back pain, thirst, bad breath, and swelling of the submandibular lymph nodes with tenderness. The tongue is coated with a white fur. At this time, if the pharyngeal cavity is examined, the palatine tonsils can be seen to be significantly swollen and congested (usually on both sides). At the location of the crypts, there are small white or light yellowish-white spots of purulent plugs. If the purulent plugs are examined under a microscope, streptococcus or staphylococcus can be seen. These small dotted purulent plugs can often combine into a membrane, covering the surface of the tonsils. The appearance is the same as diphtheria, so patients often mistake it for diphtheria and seek medical treatment from a doctor.

The course of the disease, if good, can be alleviated after a few days of treatment (such as a decrease in temperature, a reduction in pain, and the tonsils subsiding and decongesting). Complete cure usually takes about a week. However, it is common for the body temperature to suddenly rise on the second or third day after the various symptoms have subsided, and the various symptoms reappear. This is probably due to the occurrence of peritonsillar inflammation. Peritonsillar inflammation can also turn into a peritonsillar abscess. At this time, surgery must be performed to drain the pus and heal the disease. Peritonsillar inflammation and peritonsillar abscess may be described in detail in the next issue.

Speaking of the treatment of this disease, it can be divided into five points: 1. Oral medication = After a specialist physician has examined and determined the disease, quinine can be taken immediately. The dosage can be determined by the physician's prescription. I cannot arbitrarily give a certain dosage. This is determined according to age and physical condition. Its benefit is that it can shorten the course of the disease and make it easier to recover. 2. Local therapy = can be divided into three types: topical medicine, gargling medicine, and compress method. These are all matters under the guidance of a physician. 3. In the case of habitual angina, it is best to perform a tonsillectomy or removal. 4. Patients with rheumatism must tell the doctor whether they have had this disease before. Even if they have not, they should ask the doctor to examine the tonsils, because there is often a related relationship. 5. Be cautious about receiving diphtheria antitoxin injections. When I am in clinical practice, when I encounter families with patients suffering from tonsillitis, they often say, "I have already been injected with diphtheria antitoxin, why is it still not effective?" At this time, it is difficult for me to judge. I cannot say that the doctor who injected the diphtheria antitoxin is wrong, nor can I criticize the poor quality of the antitoxin. However, I hope that readers of the newspaper will pay attention to three points: A. Diphtheria antitoxin is only uniquely effective for diphtheria. It is not effective for tonsillitis. B. If a doctor wants to inject diphtheria antitoxin, it is best to rely on a microscopic examination report (that is, whether there are diphtheria bacilli). C. Patients suffering from tonsillitis who have already been injected with diphtheria antitoxin are not in any danger, only losing money and the credibility of the antitoxin. However, when injecting any antitoxin for the second time, it is best to tell the doctor, stating that they were injected with diphtheria antitoxin on such and such a date in such and such a month of such and such a year, because this can draw the doctor's attention and prevent a reaction to the antitoxin.

Little Western Paradise 203

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 1: A Carriage of Distant Guests Arrives from Guanzhong; A Penniless Family Crosses the Ferry, Lamenting the Men of Qin

By the time he recollected himself, this long stretch of road was straight and flat. In five minutes, they had already traveled six or seven *li*. He shouted, “Oh dear! I've lost my hat. Please stop the carriage.” Zhao Guofu said, “Can you ask a foreigner sitting in the front to stop the carriage?” Li Shilian said, “What's there to fear about foreigners? I see foreigners all day long in Shanghai. In the concessions, it's only the British, Americans, and French with whom diplomacy is difficult. But with White Russians, you can joke around. The Germans have no power now, what's there to fear about them?” Zhao and Wang, who both worked for Germans, were not convinced by these words. But since the European War, Germans really had no power in China. How could they deny that? So, Wang Laowu attacked from the side, asking, “If you met Japanese people, would you dare joke with them too?” Li Shilian said, “Unless I met them in Hongkou, Shanghai, where they run rampant. If I met them in the French Concession, I doubt they'd dare do anything.” After this long discourse on foreign affairs, the carriage traveled further and further, and his hat could only be sacrificed in vain, left unattended. But after being subtly ridiculed a few times by Wang Laowu, knowing that he was supporting the Germans, he thought, "These two people's thinking is truly worthy of making them traitors. Two utter snobs." Wang Laowu was also thinking, “This rash fellow is also coming to Shaanxi to look for work. If he really gets a job in Shaanxi, then that place must be three feet high in the sky.” So they looked at each other with cold eyes, and both fell silent. Zhang Jiefu, with his hands pillowed on the wooden box, was also lost in thought. Suddenly, he heard a crackling sound from the basket, not knowing what kind of glass or porcelain had broken. Then, a whiff of wine wafted toward his nose. His lifelong fondness was for a sip of wine; his nickname was "Wine-Crazy Zhang San." On this windy, dusty, sun-baked carriage, he didn’t know what to do. (5)

Traffic Light 204

— Ziyun

Red represents danger, green indicates safety.

At every intersection, traffic lights always stare like strange eyes, watching all those who come and go in the tiger's mouth-like intersection for fame and fortune.

Traffic controllers wrapped in uniforms turn off the red light and turn on the green light. Trams and cars, like armored vehicles and tanks, rush to the front lines recklessly.

Following them are bicycles, rickshaws, and finally, people hobbling on two lame legs.

From here, the authority of science is fully demonstrated. Those using electricity and motors have defeated those relying solely on mechanical things. Those hobbling on two legs are, of course, the most backward.

The green light turns off, the red light turns on, and the vehicles and pedestrians on the cross street are also in such a scene.

This is the mechanization of order at the intersection, which is the so-called "safety first."

Red represents danger, green indicates safety.

But some people cross the street under the red light, and some people bleed crimson blood and milky white brain matter at the tiger's mouth-like intersection.

Unless they are lifeless, even if they have only a trace of life left, they will be scolded as "dying unjustly" and "swine" because the red light stares like strange eyes, indicating danger long ago.

Vehicles and pedestrians on the road come and go non-stop. Red and green lights take turns indicating the safe road for people.

Traffic lights are responsible for the safety of pedestrians’ lives, serving all day long, until people rest. Only then do they slightly close those two strange eyes.

But at daybreak, the two strange eyes are open at the intersection again.

Sketch of a Small Teahouse 206

— Zhang Muliang

In the small teahouse near the vegetable market street, it is crowded with people in the evening. Under the emerald green gaslight, mostly figures from the business community are reflected, either shopkeepers or bosses. Everyone gathers to chat casually, talk about business, or make deals.

Originally, everyone came to listen to Mr. [Storyteller] tell the story of "Three Smiles," but this Mr. [Storyteller] was called to sing for a private party at Chen's mansion and couldn't get away for a while. Therefore, these listeners couldn’t avoid having to wait for a long time, and began to talk loudly, drowning out even the buzzing of the mosquitoes in the corner.

A butcher with a scraggly beard said, "In these years, schools have been very patriotic. Others don't need to be mentioned, but just take the principal of that XX Middle School. He can truly be called a patriotism expert. No matter how hot the weather is, under the scorching sun, he tears his throat and gives speeches, his head full of sweat and tears streaming down. How difficult that is!"

A bald man sitting next to him, holding a handful of watermelon seeds, scattered them on the table and chimed in, "That principal is really something. You only need to listen to him talk about boycotting Japanese goods, regaining rights, enduring hardship to restore the country, and five-minute fever. What kind of reasoning he speaks. I was very moved after hearing his words!"

They were talking loudly when a foreign goods store owner was disturbed. He ran over from the next table and asked, "Are you talking about that principal?" The butcher said, "Yes! We say he is a patriotism expert." The foreign goods store owner snorted in his nose and said, "Don't mention it! I know everything about this Mr. [Principal]. He says he doesn't buy foreign goods, but his woman cut dozens of dollars worth of printed eastern gauze in my store yesterday. The end of the month is tomorrow, and I still have to prepare to go to his door to collect the account!"

Everyone talked more and more excitedly. The eyes and ears of almost all the guests were focused on this corner. Suddenly, the sound of strings rang out with a *ding-ding-dong-dong*. It turned out that the storyteller had come on stage. Everyone wanted to listen to the story of Wang Laohu snatching the bride and what Zhou Wenbin was doing in his sister's room, so it was quiet without a sound, only slightly some sounds of eating watermelon seeds and the mosquitoes buzzing in the corner, echoing the storyteller's string music.

Records of Fleeting Fragrance from the Imperial Court 207

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

After the boned and scaled crucian carp meat was cooked with tender tofu, it was presented to the Empress Dowager for the second time: she used a silver spoon to drink several spoonfuls in a row, and at the same time praised it with audible relish, making those of us standing beside her drool. Later, she suddenly specified that half of what was left should be given to me to eat. This really made me overjoyed! Because if the Empress Dowager specified that leftovers or tea that was left over should be given to someone to eat, that person's worth would suddenly increase a lot; not only would others envy him, but he himself would also consider it an extremely honorable thing. So the Empress Dowager left half of this fresh fish soup for me to eat, which was really delightful: what's more, the taste of the fish soup cooked with tender tofu was indeed very good?

Although the Empress Dowager's appetite did not decrease as much as that of ordinary elderly people, there were so many things presented by the Imperial Kitchen that she could not finish eating or drinking everything, whether it was a bowl of dishes or a cup of soup; as a result, she developed the habit of giving the leftovers to the people who served her. However, I always dealt with this kind of grace very carefully: if she had not told me to eat or drink the leftovers, no matter how much I loved to eat or drink in my heart, I would try my best to endure it and immediately hand the original bowl or cup to the eunuchs to clean up; if she had already told me clearly to eat or drink the leftovers, then I could no longer be polite, and I must first respectfully kowtow to her to show that I was twelve minutes satisfied and grateful for her reward, and then eat and drink what was left in the bowl or cup without hesitation. No matter how full I was, I had to obey gladly, otherwise it would be violating the imperial decree, a crime that could not be pardoned. (114)

Men and Women 208

— (Shazhou)

Men have too many opportunities to suffer setbacks in these years.

To cite two simple examples: Film companies’ actresses appear one by one, and are praised and supported one by one, but what about actors? The actors' skills are not necessarily lower than those of the actresses, and the number of people working in the industry is not necessarily less than that of the actresses, but the actors who were successful in the past are now dull. Every year, schools hold queen elections and produce school flowers. Photos of the queens and school flowers are to be published in various pictorials, and outstanding female students must also be published. What about male students? Are there fewer outstanding male students than female students? But pictorials always abandon them.

But is the popularity of women a good phenomenon in society? Does the popularity of women mean that women's status has improved?

Folklore

Speech on Sacrificing to Confucius in Shanghai 209

— Shanghai General News Agency

This year, in order to promote Confucius's deeds and to express reverence, the central government specially proposed the 132nd Standing Committee Meeting, which decided that August 27th would be the anniversary of the birth of the first teacher Confucius, and issued a notice to all local party and government agencies to prepare for the commemoration. On that day, the Municipal Party Department will jointly convene representatives from all walks of life in conjunction with the Municipal Government to hold a memorial meeting in the Dacheng Hall of the Nanjing "Temple of Literature." On the one hand, in order to show solemnity, the National Government specially dispatched member Ye Chucang to Qufu to preside over the sacrifice on that day, and each of the five institutes and the two departments of education sent members to accompany the sacrifice. -- Originally, the "Ding Sacrifice" of sacrificial rites is to be seen again today.

Speaking of the sacrificial ceremony to Confucius in Shanghai, the "Wenmiao Ding Sacrifice Manual" has always been used as the standard. This manual is based on the Liling Ding Sacrifice Manual obtained by Shanghai gentry Wang Qingxun. In the Tongzhi year of Wuchen [1868], Su Aiding Richang published the manual in the provincial capital, and even the plates were collected and submitted, and stored in the Zunjing Pavilion. Later, it was reprinted after cleaning. At the end of the Guangxu era, the Ding Sacrifice was promoted to a major sacrifice, and the Ministry issued a martial dance manual. Its rituals, offerings, and music and dance aspects were slightly different from before, but Shanghai County "did not bother to change it." In the third year of the Republic of China [1914], the Ritual System Hall of the Department of Political Affairs issued diagrams of the sacrificial rites and costumes of Confucius, and the rituals and costumes were even more different than before. Therefore, Ding Xicheng, the director-general of the then Public Funds and Public Directors Management Office, together with Lin Zengyu, the custodian of the Temple of Literature, etc., deliberated on the past and present, planned the gains and losses, and the sacrificial rites of Confucius were splendidly complete. By the thirteenth year of the Republic of China [1924], Fan Yinshen, the director of music and dance at the Shanghai Confucius Temple, deeply aware that the situation had changed and the old Wenmiao Ding Sacrifice Manual was no longer completely applicable (and its plates were destroyed in the chaos of the Republic of China, leaving only one or two isolated copies), he began to compile the "Shanghai Sea Sacrifice Confucius Manual" with reference to the sacrificial rites of Confucius. The book was completed in half a year, and was published by the Sanitation Bureau in the summer of the fourteenth year of the Republic of China [1925].

According to the "Shanghai Sacrifice Confucius Manual," we will look at the style of the sacrificial rites of Confucius in Shanghai:

(1) Announcer - The main offering official, the sub-offering official, and the accompanying ceremonial officials take their positions one after another, and the ritual correction official ascends the steps to correct the rituals. Open the door to welcome the gods, raise the welcoming music, and kneel and bow four times to participate in the gods. Then present silk and wine to perform the first offering ceremony, raise the first offering music, and kneel and bow four times. The Martial Merit Dance retreats, and the Literary Virtue Dance advances. Perform the sub-offering ceremony, raise the sub-offering music. Perform the final offering ceremony, until the final offering music, and kneel and bow four times. The scribe holds the blessings, the silk official holds the silk, the wine official invites the wine, and the food official invites the food and respectfully sends them to the pyre. Close the door and the ceremony is completed.

(2) Musical Rhythm - Before the sacrifice, strike the Jin drum 360 times to warn. (Strike three times) After the musicians and dancers have taken their places under the steps, the shift drum is sounded. (There are thirteen sections in the drum score) The singers hold the tablets, the musicians hold the instruments and follow the flag in single file; the dancers hold the shields and axes and follow the rhythm in single file, advancing from both sides of the music rack in order, and each takes its place to welcome the gods. The Dacheng bells and drums sound together, and then the music is joined (there are six chapters in the music). The Welcome Gods play the Zhaohe chapter. The First Offering plays the Lihe chapter, and dances the Lihe dance. (First set) The Sub-Offering plays the Xihe chapter, and dances the Xihe dance. (Second set) The Final Offering plays the Yuanhe chapter, and dances the Yuanhe dance. (Third set) The Retreat Offering plays the Changhe chapter. Sending the Gods plays the Dehe chapter. Each time a chapter is played, the flag bearer raises the flag and sings loudly: The music plays the chapter of so-and-so. The sound should rise vigorously. The first two words are read, and the last four words are arranged evenly, the long rhyme gradually increases, the spring appearance is harmonious and elegant, the ending is long, and then strike the blessing three times to start the music.

(3) Dacheng Hall Blessing Text - There is a certain format, always: "Thinking that the first teacher's virtue participates in creation, and the Tao penetrates the past and the present. Collecting the great achievements of the sages, illuminating the former knowledge to set an example. The world is for the public, the measure of one person in China; what the people have never had before, the heart of the Six Classics for thousands of years. Following the palace walls to admire the beauty, entering the room and ascending the hall; offering sacrifices with respect, first understanding and then following the law, now…"

(4) Dacheng Hall Furnishings - There are nine kinds of sacrificial vessels: *jue* (wine cup), *bian* (bamboo container), *fu* (square sacrificial vessel), *gui* (round sacrificial vessel), *dou* (wooden stand), *xing* (cauldron), *fei* (basket), *zu* (altar), *deng* (pedestal); in addition to the Taigeng and Hegeng, there are thirty-two kinds of sacrificial offerings, and the setting position is divided into six rows. The Taigeng, which is loaded in the "Deng," is in the center of the fourth row, and the sheep, cattle, and pigs in the six rows of "Zu" face the three jade *jue* in the first row.

(5) Musicians' and Dancers' Costumes - The crown is black silk (or cotton), and the pure edges are all black with gold leaf (in each provincial place, the pure edges of the musicians and dancers do not use gold leaf), blue tassels without threads, the covering plate uses a square style, and the front, rear, left, and right are all placed flat with pointed corners. The crown badge is square, one inch in length and width, made of gilded copper, engraved with the seal characters "Music" and "Dance" in positive relief. The clothes are made of blue silk (or cotton), long to the ankles, and the width is each body; the sleeves are longer than the hands; the cuffs are six inches; the two overlaps of the sleeves are like straight collars; the collars and lower ends are all black edges for two guards: the collar pleats are from a flipped style, the waist pleats are behind, and the fat and thinness are about to be tied with a ribbon; the whole body continues to have small sunflower patterns. (Musicians and dancers in each provincial place are not embroidered). (To be continued)

Economic Special Issue

Recent Shanghai Call Loan Interest Rates 210

— Wei Youfei

The call loan interest rate is a yardstick for measuring the supply and demand situation in the Shanghai financial market. Before the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan, this term was called "silver call loan." There was also a separate term, "foreign call loan," for the lending rate of silver dollars at that time, but now it has been unified. Its meaning is to calculate the daily interest rate per thousand yuan.

There are two types of Shanghai call loan rates: one set by the Banking Joint Reserve Committee and the other in the money changers' guild market. Due to historical and customary reasons, the former's check clearing situation is far inferior to the latter, with its clearing amount only one-fifth of the latter's. Even in general business circles and Chinese banks, the call loan rate set by the money changers' guild market is mostly used as the standard, so this article is based on the latter.

In the "silver call loan" era, the Shanghai Money Changers' Guild's business rules stipulated that the silver call loan rate should not exceed seven qian. Now it is stipulated that the call loan interest rate should not be higher than seven jiao. Looking back four or five years ago, a call loan interest rate of four or five qian was common, and it often reached the maximum limit when finances were active. However, after the January 28th Incident, the economic organization of Shanghai, and of the country, suffered a significant blow. At the same time, due to the impact of the international economic downturn, the financial situation changed to sluggishness, while the banking business showed a vigorous trend in reverse. The so-called prosperity of the banking business does not refer to its own development, but is caused by the lack of outlets for funds. Those who benefited from financial adjustments were not merchants, rural areas, or general enterprises, but the banks themselves. To ensure their own safety, banks were often unwilling to lend more to general entrepreneurs. At the same time, those entrepreneurs who could stand firm, because of the reduced scope of their businesses, did not need loans. As for the fledgling industries that were weathering the storm, they were in need of funds, but the banks were unwilling to release them. As a result of this stalemate, finance often stretched and contracted in a state of relaxation. The call loan situation in Shanghai in recent years and recently is a clear proof:

Monthly Average Call Loan Interest Rate Table (Unit: Fen)

January February March April May

Year 20 13 1 2 2 4

Year 21 13 35 19 13 6

Year 22 2 1 4 4 5

Year 23 5 1 3 4 7

The reason why the period between January and February was relatively higher was because it coincided with the Lunar New Year, and according to old customs, the use of silver dollars in the market was relatively more frequent. Therefore, to statistically analyze this year's business situation, January or February should actually be included in the previous year.

Excluding January, this year's call loan market situation has the lowest average, except for the 20th year. Opening the market situation statistics, we can see that the call loan interest rate is in a stable state, with very few sudden rises or sudden drops. In addition to summarizing the old tune of "economic recession," we can also use the conclusion of evaluating the prices of general commodities: supply is high, and demand is low. First, let's talk about the supply side.

Because Shanghai is an international trading port, those in the interior who want to purchase goods must bring funds to Shanghai. Also, because of its special organization, general wealthy merchants and gentry come to Shanghai to avoid the dangers of their hometowns. These two factors are the simplest reasons for the increase in the source of funds. Below is a statistic on the flow of cash.

Shanghai Cash Flow Situation (Unit: Thousand Yuan)

The cash mentioned in the table above includes cash, silver dollars, and large bars. According to this table, there is a common point, that is, in Shanghai, the inflow and outflow of cash from and to the domestic market is often in a surplus position, while the opposite is true for foreign countries. If we compare the amount of cash flowing in from the domestic market with the amount of cash flowing out to foreign countries, the former often exceeds the latter. Therefore, Shanghai's reserves are relatively increased. However, this table cannot, of course, be regarded as a completely accurate statistic, because private exports are not included.

Another opposite trend is that the inflow of cash from the domestic market to Shanghai has an increasing trend, while the outflow from Shanghai to foreign countries has a decreasing trend. Regarding the former, we can see the signs of economic decline in the interior in recent years. In normal times, the trade situation between Shanghai and the interior is that Shanghai sends industrial products to the interior, while the interior sends agricultural products and semi-finished products to Shanghai. Therefore, the balance of payments will not be too far apart. Once the rural areas decline, there is no source for production, but consumption cannot be reduced too much. Therefore, the gap between the two sides' income and expenditure becomes wider and wider. In order to make up for this gap, the interior has to transport cash to Shanghai.

Also, because of the economic decline in the interior and the weak purchasing power, the import side of international trade has also weakened at the same time. However, a trade deficit is still a trade deficit, so the amount of cash exported to foreign countries has to be reduced.

A corresponding confirmation is to check the situation of international trade. In recent years, international trade, whether import or export, has been gradually decreasing. The decrease in imports has become a cause of the sluggish use of silver. In normal times, the interior would bring cash to Shanghai, and Shanghai would use cash to transport goods to foreign countries. Now, the cash coming from the interior is increasing, but the outlet is decreasing, thus forming a stagnant situation. Below is a comparison of the international trade situation.

Comparison of International Trade Situation (Unit: Thousand Yuan) 211

According to this situation, the supply side is large, but the outlet, whether foreign countries have no need, and domestic production circles are dispirited and lifeless. In the past, the most active season for finance in Jiangzhe financial sector was the silkworm season, but in recent years, the so-called national industry of silkworm reeling has shown a distinctly bleak situation, especially this year. In 1930, someone statistically calculated that there were 105 silk factories in Shanghai, with 25,066 silk reeling machines, while this year there are only 33 factories, with 7,510 silk reeling machines, accounting for only three-tenths of the 1930 figure. Even in terms of prices, the highest price for improved breed superior cocoons is no more than 35 yuan, and the lowest is no more than 20 yuan. Compared with the recent last year's market price of 44 yuan at the highest and 25 yuan at the lowest, it is obvious how the silk industry is struggling in distress.

Secondly, the relatively developed textile and silk weaving industries also show signs of decline.

On the surface, it seems that the financial situation is an excess of floating capital, a state of stagnation, but it is not. In the declining production sector, there is actually a need for financial assistance, but it is useless. Because of the decline in the production sector, the financial industry does not dare to lend recklessly for safety reasons; the production sector further reduces its scope because it cannot obtain turnover from the financial sector. This situation is harmful to both.

The excessively low call loan interest rate is not a matter of concern, because low interest rates can reduce the costs of all production sectors. However, under today's circumstances, the depressed state of the call loan interest rate shows the powerlessness, fatigue, and lack of vitality of the production sector, which is not only a fatal injury to the financial industry, but also a pessimistic phenomenon for the production sector.

The Alarming Decline in Shanghai Raw Silk Exports 212

— Ling Wenqin

The sluggishness of Shanghai's raw silk exports began in the late autumn of 1931. Since then, there have been no large orders. Although there have been sporadic transactions, they are all filled with spot goods, and the price is reduced for competitive sales. The market situation has therefore declined, and manufacturers are crying out in misery. Later, the government provided relief by issuing public bonds, which allowed for a slight recovery. In the spring of 1932, the Japanese invaded Shanghai, and war broke out, causing the silk market to stagnate for three months. There were some transactions in the summer, mostly to sell off inventories at a reduced price, with market prices between 550 and 650 taels per dan. However, it did not last long, and fatigue reappeared, with vitality declining day by day. In the spring of 1933, the government encouraged exports, subsidizing factory-reeled silk by 100 taels per dan, paid in public bonds, which ended at the end of May. Exports saw a slight improvement. However, the essential panic of the silk industry remained as before. Except for the upper-level manufacturers and speculators who enjoyed this benefit, the vast majority did not get a piece of the pie. In the summer of that year, affected by the US recovery policy, market prices rose, with sales prices ranging from over 800 yuan to 1,000 yuan (raw silk prices also abolished taels and adopted the yuan), and many transactions were made, gradually showing a glimmer of hope. However, it did not last long, and it returned to its former state. Not only were transactions scarce, but prices also became cheaper day by day. Ordinary goods had fallen to 570 or 580 yuan by the end of the year, a huge difference of one-third. Most of our country's manufacturers have weak capital, leading to flight and escape, and there are many instances of this. Before the new cocoons came on the market this spring, the price was around 500 yuan. Unexpectedly, since the new goods entered the market, there have been no transactions, and prices have also been weakening day by day. Recently, the market situation for ordinary, coarse silk is only worth 420 or 430 yuan, and the scarcity of transactions is a new record unseen since the export of raw silk in our country. Because June, July, and August have always been the peak months for exports, but this year it is quiet and leisurely, which is beyond expectations. It is estimated that from June 1 to August 15 of this year, only 983 bales of white factory-reeled silk were shipped to Europe and 903 bales to the Americas. During the same period last year, 3,258 bales were shipped to Europe and 5,570 bales to the Americas. The most pitiful yellow factory-reeled silk has only 10 bales shipped to Europe so far. During the same period last year, 1,691 bales were shipped to Europe and 1,585 bales to the Americas. In total, since June of this year, only 4,419 bales of various raw silk have been exported, compared to 15,557 bales during the same period last year. This is a reduction of about two-thirds. According to this calculation, the output of white factory-reeled silk this year will be within 10,000 bales. I don't know how our silk industry will handle the aftermath. Moreover, the Sichuan silk in yellow factory-reeled silk is encountering particularly difficult circumstances. Not only is there still a large amount of inventory, but new silk is also being produced continuously, and its situation is several times more difficult than that of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The export quantities of various raw silk in Shanghai in the past ten years are listed below.

(Note) X includes Africa

Shanghai's raw silk exports have always occupied an important position in foreign trade and are closely related to the national economy. Before the first half of 1931, although there were ups and downs in exports over the years, it was still possible to maintain its inherent position. Moreover, in terms of selling price, ordinary goods were all above 900 taels or 1,000 taels. From 1928 to 1930, it was the golden age of the industry. All parts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang also competed to set up silk factories at that time. The silver and money industry welcomed loans for silkworm cocoons because they were short-term and easy to sell, unlike the sluggishness of other industries. Who would have known that today's silkworm cocoons would fall into a slump to this point? Looking back on the past, one cannot help but feel emotional. Fortunately, domestic silk factories have recently adopted factory-reeled silk, which can sell about 30,000 dans per year. The domestic silk factories have also made a great contribution to the silk factory industry being able to survive until now. The causes and consequences of its failure are classified below, so that readers may gain additional reference beyond idealization.

(1) White Factory Silk - My country's factory silk has been famous in Europe and America for many years. Since Japan saw it and became envious, it engaged in research and development, constantly improving it, and sent a large number of experts to visit silk-using countries, with the purpose of catering to the psychology of buyers. After returning, they engaged in mass production to meet the needs of the world. Since the United States adopted uniform inspection, Japanese silk gradually rose to prominence. After experts invented new cost-saving equipment, the effect was remarkable. Since 1931, they have also used exchange rate dumping, and exports have greatly increased. The Shanghai-US market was defeated. Japanese silk began dumping in Europe during the Shanghai war. Europe has always disliked Japanese silk, but it used various propaganda and provided its high-end products for people to try, which was then bewitching. After several experiments, it was found that the quality was indeed good, the cut ends were less, and it was very suitable for use, and the price was particularly low. The raw silk of China and Italy was greatly affected. Today, Japanese silk has entered the inner sanctum in Europe. The reasons for the failure of Shanghai factory silk are nothing more than the following points: (A) Too many leaders, that is, gathering 120,000 capital, and those without experience and knowledge become managers, making rough and shoddy products based on personal will, without knowing how to communicate with each other, research and improve, and the market situation rises and falls, leaving it to fate. (B) High-end products must wait for huge debts before they are willing to sell them, without considering the trend of the world market. (C) The products are uneven, and there are too many brands. Each brand cannot supply a large amount of goods, and each batch of products is different. (This point is related to the declining quality of raw materials. There have been successes in improving silkworm rearing, which should be improved.) (D) The Italian-style silk reeling machines from decades ago have not been changed, which is very uneconomical for modern production and consumption. (E) Exporters are overly critical, and use improper means to sell the goods, resulting in total failure. In short, the declining quality of Chinese silk and the high price are the main reasons.

In order to recover lost ground, the silk industry and the silkworm industry must work together to be effective. (A) If a certain factory in Wuxi has achieved success, there should be at least a dozen or so organizations of the same type, and it is best to jointly set up a research department for improvement, so that it can keep pace with Japan. However, this organization is very expensive. In the first few years, or in the event of a world economic panic, it cannot make a profit. It must be maintained by the government or given various conveniences, so that those in charge can do their best to succeed. (B) Establish higher silk-making schools to train management talent for silk factories. (C) Train foreign trade personnel in raw silk for direct export. (D) The goods reeled by each factory must be submitted to the Commodity Inspection Bureau for strict inspection, classification, and certification to facilitate transactions. Those who fail the inspection are only allowed to be sold domestically and are absolutely not allowed to be exported.

(2) Yellow Factory Silk - My country's yellow factory silk has always been mainly sold to Europe, with few exports to the United States. Since it has been subjected to competition and low-price dumping by Japan and Italy, we have failed. Its advantages and disadvantages are roughly the same as those of white factory silk. However, the Sichuan yellow silk has a huge output, and the risk is also the greatest.

(3) Qi Li Silk - Qi Li silk entered the road of decline ten years ago. The Xunzhen merchants are ignorant of the world situation, and its market in Europe and the United States has been occupied by rayon, so there are not many exports. As for India and Africa, it will also decrease in the future, mainly because India's tariffs have increased, and the coarse silk of Guangdong is very suitable for local needs, and the price is also low. Therefore, Guangdong silk exports to India and other places will be prosperous. At present, Japanese lower-grade products are also being test-marketed, but the results are average.

(4) Yellow Silk and Yellow Tu Silk - This silk is unique to my country and is sold to backward countries such as India and Africa. In recent years, affected by the world economic recession and India's tariffs, exports have greatly decreased. If the rulers of these imperialist countries introduce scientific knowledge and gradually advance the natives, this type of goods will undoubtedly fall into decline.

(5) Gray Silk (i.e. Pressed Silkworm Silk) - This is a special product of the Northeast. It has always relied mainly on US sales. France and Italy in Europe do not purchase much and still use it, but the large customer, the United States, has switched to using rayon instead. Since the September 18th Incident, most of these goods have been shipped to Japan. The Japanese use it to interweave with raw silk due to its low price to make silk fabrics, which are transported to Europe, Australia, and Nanyang, in very large quantities. Therefore, the exports in Shanghai are only one-tenth of what they were at their peak. If the Northeast is not recovered one day, there is no need to talk about it.

Officials and civilians in our country, seeing this silk industry crisis, talk about relief every day. Various facilities do not focus on reality, but make empty words. The silk industry itself has no practical benefits. And the silk industry groups only know to ask the government to issue public bonds to save their temporary thoughts, and have no plans or fighting spirit for their own future. I dare to say loudly that China's silk industry needs urgent scientific relief. Those who preside over it should be upright, honest, and possess deep silk knowledge, and be rich in world market experience in order to be competent. If you only engage in propaganda and do not act, the future of my country's silk industry will not know to what extent it will be corrupted.

Finally, I would like to report that Japanese mulberry fields are gradually tending to be converted into cotton fields. The experiment has been successful, and investment is currently being made in planting. Agricultural experts have also invented a method of converting silkworm cocoons into rayon wool, which will reduce the import of Australian wool by 140 million yen per year in the future. In other words, the Japanese are also looking for various outlets for their silk industry. I hope that people in our country will pay attention to it.

Finance Foreign Market Has Returned to Normal 214

Call Loan Rate Returns to Seven Percent... Silver Coins Fluctuate in Value

Since the export of silver cash, the foreign market was once tense, but the situation only eased the day before yesterday. The foreign exchange market call loan rate was three percent lower than the day before, returning to seven percent, thus returning to its former state. Call loan transactions: more than 3.4 million in morning session transfers and new transactions, more than 300,000 in afternoon session transactions, more than 500,000 in small general association transactions, and only more than 1 million in foreign mortgage transactions for redemption and new transactions. Bank collection and delivery were completely halted due to Sunday. Only money houses had more than 37 million in foreign public bill collections and deliveries and more than 600,000 in remittances from various sources. The auxiliary currency market conditions fluctuated. Jiangnan small silver coins were difficult to exchange, suddenly falling four yuan, calculated at 833 yuan in both the morning and afternoon sessions. Guangdong small silver coin transactions were still considered good, opening half a yuan higher in the morning session, at 839 yuan. The afternoon session added another seven jiao, making 739 yuan and seven jiao, resulting in a price 1.2 yuan better than the previous day. The volume of transactions was 60,000 jiao in the morning session and 55,000 jiao in the afternoon session. Copper coins were 327,500 wen, an increase of 500 wen compared to the previous day, with a transaction price of 7,800 foreign yuan, equivalent to 25,545 strings of cash.

Securities Government Bonds Plunge Last Week 215

Loose and Excessive Chips Form Short Squeeze

Falling from One Yuan to Three or Four Yuan

Last week, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was in the final week of August futures. Due to poor conditions and loose and excessive chips, a short squeeze formed, which was only seen in recent months. Previously, the upcoming implementation of the bank savings regulations was seen as a positive sign according to common theory, and the market was crowded with bulls. However, due to the outflow of cash, high foreign call loan rates, tight credit, and banks hedging, most did not swap, coupled with rampant rumors and the Russo-Japanese situation showing signs of war, the bulls were greatly hit. Those who exited the market did so, and those who swapped did so. The market price trend was downward, differing from the highest price by a minimum of four or five yuan and a maximum of eight or nine yuan. The trend has not yet formally rebounded. A rebound is inevitable and must wait for credit to loosen before the market price naturally rises. Currently, it is only a temporary setback. The current situation has brewed into a situation where retail investors are stronger than large investors, so the future still has great fluctuations. Last week's experience: Monday was the busiest trading day, with more than 42 million in two sessions, setting a new record for the highest number of transactions. The market price plummeted due to the exit of large bull investors, falling sharply by six or seven jiao to as much as two yuan and eight or nine jiao. On Tuesday, purchases of No. 4 and No. 41 were very active, and there were also reports of new hedging transactions. The outflow of cash has attracted the attention of the government and the financial community, and there should be countermeasures to stop it soon. The market price suddenly rebounded, rising half a yuan to two yuan. On Wednesday, there was considerable competition between bulls and bears. The market price rose and fell sharply, rising one yuan in the first session, falling one yuan or even 1.6 yuan in the second session, and rising one yuan in the third session, fluctuating uncertainly, making it unpredictable. The result was slightly better. Thursday was stable, and transactions also decreased, slightly better by three or four jiao. On Friday, some bulls still exited the market, turning to a decline of several jiao to 1.5 or 6 yuan. Saturday was extremely chaotic, mostly in a short squeeze, continuing to a small decline of two or three jiao to eight or nine jiao. The market price for the week resulted in a decline of one yuan and several jiao to about 3.5 yuan. The trend thereafter should not lead to a major decline in the short term. Even if the financial community does not hedge, it will not have any impact. The total transaction volume is 17,409,500 yuan. Cotton Yarn 216

Rain in US Drought Area

Cotton Market Falls 15 Points

Yesterday, US cotton was weak due to rain in the drought area and reduced buying and selling. As a result, spot prices fell 15 points, and futures fell 13 to 18 points. British cotton futures rose 2 points. Indian cotton was soft due to speculator selling and bull liquidation. As a result, Pingguoer fell 2.5 jiao. Aomula and Bailuoxi rose 2.5 jiao. Grains Zhuanqiao New Indica Rice Arrived Yesterday in Two Loads 217

-Opening at 13 Yuan 3 Jiao-

(South of Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from various gangs were only 13 or 14 (with a total of more than 2,000 shi of goods), but most of them were late rice, and a few were thick indica rice. The sales market was still sluggish. Due to the drought, people's hearts were high. If the price of thick indica rice and late rice increased by 2 or 3 jiao, Duyangjian would rise by 1 jiao. As for Yinbian Yuan, the market was completely devoid of goods. As for new indica rice, in addition to the increasing amount of Changdong new rice by 3 jiao, Zhuanqiao new indica rice also started to be sold on the market today, with three loads arriving, about 200 shi. Because the goods were pure, the price was the same as that of Dongxin, opening at 12 yuan 3 jiao to 2.5 jiao.

(North of Shanghai) Yesterday, there were more than ten sources from various routes in Hexia. The various goods on the market, such as Quwei white indica rice, were flat, early thin rice slightly liquified, Baiyuan and various sharp varieties continued to be traded. The market situation was that white indica rice and thin rice were stable, early rice and Baiyuan were tight, and various sharp varieties were slightly tight. Dongxin indica rice was scarce and sold well, and the price trend was graceful.

Metals Activities at the Huisi Iron Factory's Sales Increase 218

Since the sluggish sales of Huisi iron from foreign gangs, the market has been depressed. In recent days, the factory's sales market has suddenly moved, and the standard, under the influence of the sharp increase in foreign pricing, has also moved upward. For example, old steel factory goods are estimated at 30 yuan per box, new steel factory goods are estimated at 29 yuan, and Yeji goods are opened at 28 yuan and 5 jiao, all of which have risen by 5 jiao to 1 yuan. However, local factories in this port have all dumped futures and spot goods. It is said that 2,600 to 2,700 boxes have been reached in two days. Foreign gangs such as Qingdao, Tianjin, and Fujian gangs have also added a lot of supplies.
