Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao

Talks

Christmas Message 219

— Wen

This year, the birth of the late teacher Confucius will be more lively than any Christmas in the past ten years or so. In this country where everything is believed in fate, the fate of Confucius's spirit in heaven, its prosperity and decline, can only be sought in the cycle of the sexagenary cycle.

Originally, in China, a poor and simple cultural and academic field, Confucius had his immortal position. The bad thing is that the disciples of the sage for thousands of years only knew to use "Confucius said..." and so on as a stepping stone for the professional movement of bookworms, just like Christians "eating the Bible." More than 90% of Confucius's believers also "eat the Five Classics." Since the purpose is limited to "eating," naturally there is no discussion of criticism, creation, and promotion. Moreover, the ideological rule of successive "political sages" after Emperor Wu of Han and the "closed-door vehicle building" of scholars in the Han Dynasty and Neo-Confucianists in the Song Dynasty finally turned Confucius's thought into a "nameless swelling poison" that has been a mystery for thousands of years. This is certainly the misfortune of Confucius's spirit in heaven, but especially the bad luck of the literati and intellectuals of past generations. Because they have eaten "Confucius's rice" for thousands of years, but nineteen have never recognized Confucius from the lines of "Book of Songs" and "Confucius said."

The misfortune of Confucius's thought really started with the May Fourth New Culture Movement. Chen Duxiu, the old general who is regarded as "deeply sinful" by many people and is still facing official lawsuits, and Wu Yu, the old hero who "single-handedly attacked the Confucius shop," have made very profound criticisms of Confucius's thought. In all fairness, this cannot but be regarded as a major advancement in China's academic and ideological circles. Because there must be criticism before there can be progress, and some valuable parts of Confucius's philosophy and political thought can withstand criticism. However, that work of re-evaluating Confucius's thought was met with the frantic opposition of the guardians of the Tao. When opposition was ineffective, it was followed by rumors, and Chen Duxiu became the advocate of "licentiousness as the first of all virtues and filial piety as the first of all evils."

The "adversity comes to an end and prosperity begins" of Confucius's deity or the language of the Confucian Temple has really started in recent years. Two years ago, one or two people who were worried about the world and wanted to correct people's hearts and stop evil words wore formal attire or Zhongshan suits and used the music of the yellow bell and great lu and the sacrifice of the whole pig to worship Confucius. Then, the dikes of etiquette such as men and women swimming separately, banning "dating," and banning gaudy costumes also arose in response to the times. These works may have given some blows to the modern movement, and the lively drama of splashing corrosive liquid and "fascinating to death" was also convenient for some journalists.

However, the most solemn and regarded as a grand ceremony is naturally the Confucius worship movement in the style of 1934, almost with bells and drums ringing and the phoenixes reappearing. The Confucian birthday, which is a grand occasion for a while, is only something that I am not sensitive to, and I have some opinions to explain incidentally.

First, the respect for Confucius is definitely not in the form. Chinese people, from large politics to small friendships, all make use of "formalism." To respect Confucius and focus on what music to use, what rituals to perform, and guide unified rituals is nothing more than a manifestation of formalism. In fact, what Mr. Confucius in heaven needs is probably to focus on the criticism and review of his theories and thoughts, so as to obtain greater progress and development. Otherwise, the set of being posthumously named King Wenxuan and honored as the Great Accomplishment Supreme Sage has long been practiced by emperors of past dynasties, and now it should be. Only by extracting its immortal part and examining and selecting what is not applicable to the twentieth century can we strive for the rational existence of the Confucian way. I believe that Confucius, who is as intelligent and sensible as Confucius, if he knew after death, would definitely understand the truth of "Aufhebung."

Second, that whole set of "Confucius said" cannot be used as a political incantation. The so-called "literary light shoots at the Dipper" was originally a kind of mad ravings of ancient talented scholars and literati. In modern times, in the war crisis where every gap between countries is filled with the smell of gunpowder, what can "shoot" is definitely not "literary light" but cannons and machine guns. Respecting Confucius is only to show respect for the succession of academic culture and the enlightenment of future generations. If you rely on respecting Confucius as an incantation, you will inevitably suffer the most tragic failure. The reason is the simplest: "small regular script sheep hair" or "seven purple three sheep" are after all swept on paper and cannot be used as anti-aircraft guns.

Apart from the above two points, which I regard as a taboo of the Confucius worship movement, I sincerely raise my hands to approve of promoting the sacred way. "Great is Confucius"!

Piano Lesson 220

— Yi An

Miscellany 221

— Bing

Proudhon once said such a sentence: "Property is theft," this is a famous saying, no, it is the ultimate truth. Since the formation of the private property system to this day, the endless disputes in society, if we do not have some selfishness, probably everyone thinks it is related to property. In the current society where the private property system exists, natural property has supreme authority. Precisely because of this, students must calculate how to get promoted and make a fortune in the future, and officials must love to scrape people's fat and ointment. And so on, other industry, commerce and hundreds of industries, also invariably diligently seek profits. If we look at these with intuition, we will of course not discover its wrong points, and think that it is a reasonable behavior in life, and at most we will say "greed obscures the mind." In fact, it is greatly wrong, but it is a blatant act of theft. People only say that those who steal are thieves, but in fact, like the above-mentioned ordinary people, that is, all people in the current society, are not all possessing the heart of thieves? Those who are wealthy, which one is not a thief? If you see this point clearly, you will know more than half of the society.

Truth is not easy to find, because it is limited by time and space. In other words, it is indeed the truth at this time, but it will become non-truth at another time; it is the truth in this place, but it becomes non-truth in another place. For example, thirty years ago, the three obediences and four virtues of Chinese women, foot binding and hair accumulation were the truth, but today, not only is it not the truth, but it has suffered infinite contempt. Chinese people use burial for the dead is the truth, but the Japanese do not think so, and only cremation is considered the truth. There are countless such examples. I think only the sentence "beauty is in the eye of the beholder" and this kind of fact are the unchanging truth, no matter when or where, a man or a woman will always feel that his or her beloved lover is like a unique flower.

Sichuan's land tax has been pre-collected to the 68th year of the Republic of China, which is a good phenomenon, and I have no complaints. It's just that I am a little uneasy in my heart, because I wonder if this current Republic of China has such a "longevity"? If not, then I really don't know how this account will be calculated in the future?…

According to reports, more than 50 counties in Hunan Province reported disasters of "hopeless autumn harvest," and Zhejiang Province estimated that this year's autumn harvest would be at most 30%. I respectfully record the summary here for the reference of people living in the comfortable nest of Shanghai.

Record of Abstaining from Dancing 222

— Dao

Wandering in the metropolis, living a single life, what is the way to spend the lonely heart and the lonely days? So I sank into the ballroom. Using a lonely heart to squeeze into that not lonely place, although it will often make the feeling of loneliness even stronger. But hearing the light and lively music, and the fleshy women, the shadow of loneliness will temporarily leave my side, and drop my lonely soul.

After a long time, it becomes a kind of addiction, like being addicted to smoking. Whenever I feel bored and dull in the house, my legs will instinctively slide into these places. I can't even guess that if I don't go, I will feel empty and unfulfilled as if my soul has been pulled out. But when I go, I don't necessarily dance. Sometimes I order a cup of clear tea, sit half asleep, endlessly, until dawn, and run out without dancing a single dance.

In this way, I am suffering from severe evening sickness. Doing day as night and night as day, life completely loses its angle. Once night falls and the lights come on, my demonic thoughts follow and blossom, and I turn into a ghostly night wanderer in the style of a dipsomaniac.

But that kind of prosperous scene is always separated from me by a thick membrane. I have never had any deep interest. Crossing out of that green glass door, returning home alone, the lonely heart still returns to loneliness, and it has not diminished. And I am sinking more and more into melancholy.

But why do this? Life is worth cherishing. That kind of licentious life is simply equal to chronic suicide. You can't lightly ruin yourself like this! You must understand that those women all have a sweet mouth that specializes in lying, and every dimple is filled with the stench of copper rust. All the joy is built on top of gold. Moreover, these places are not places I can go at all. They are just labyrinths for people who are full and idle, with flesh shells but no feelings. I should be a person with feelings, but why should I mix with people who have no feelings?

So I began to feel sorry for the shamelessness of my life. There are many ways to pass the time, but I chose this decadent place. I must make up my mind to cut off this evil thought. Otherwise, I am a zero survivor. Therefore, in the future, when I stumble into the ballroom, I will add to the degree of disgust each time, and try my best to think from other aspects, so that the components of hatred and contempt are expanded as much as possible. Make my mood gradually separated from the object in front of me.

Regard all women as poisonous snakes, as ghosts covered with gorgeous colored clothes, wriggling in the dark lamplight, secretly sucking that essence. But people are all fascinated by that alluring smile and have not noticed the ugly and hideous face hidden inside the colored clothes.

And the more I look, the clearer I see, and I shiver with goosebumps all over my body, which scares me and moves me. Finally, I escape as if escaping for my life, turn my head back, and glance at the people left behind who are still happily sending themselves into the mud pit, which is really pitiful and laughable. On the one hand, I am happy to get rid of the bad environment, and all of a sudden I spit out the heavy depression trapped in my heart, and take another breath of fresh air.

From then on, I recognized it as a demon cave and never wanted to go again.

(Literature and Art)

Ballad of a Young Master 223

— Bai Jiao

Gao Tang is not a dream, the warm fragrance is near, gold is used to buy laughter and kisses, the world is not surprised by the red rouge, the new bamboo in the village also spreads powder, the young master is rich and generous, every night in the singing building he embraces a dancing waist, he loves to listen to new voices especially fast, (the new voice is named Express Train, describing the recent trend of mutual attraction between men and women), since ancient times the golden house is suitable for hiding beauty, oaths are made and then abandoned, the two feelings are like glue, Wenjun does not write a white-headed song, the young master specializes in socializing, Austin is ten miles away in the foreign field, speaking Western languages, he is English and handsome, dressed up as a world (the Western suit brand is World) people envy him, throwing fruit, Panlang is suspected of being reborn, the beauties in the sea of gold consumption are gorgeous, social interactions are open and there are no taboos, since ancient times the young master is called carefree, he does not believe that there is disappointment in the world, old love is big and bulky, new love is a celestial fairy, meeting by chance is like glue, separate dwellings are built on both sides, the father hears this and is furious, the mother is still tolerant and understands the mistake of socializing, in an instant new love becomes old love, it is not necessarily that the moth eyebrows are jealous, why did they not marry early in those years, how could there be no graceful woman from a famous family, better to die than to be unfree, the young master is affectionate and does not discuss it, new love and old love, traces are cut off, there are flowers and honey everywhere, remarriage is a crime if there is no marriage, the white eyes and gold are about to break, is it not true that Deng's copper mountain is empty, a life of sweetness and hardship in romance, the unparalleled luxury has become a dream of the past, the descendants of the princes are pitifully destitute, wandering in the streets in despair and speechless, hungry in another country, tears like rain, afraid to say his real name when meeting people, dew cannot quench hunger and stones are difficult to cook, how can you know the difficulty of farming, yesterday's death and today's life should be too late, who gets the deer when the Zheng people lose the deer, do not remember the red lights and green wine times. (Not compensated)

(Letter) To the esteemed editors of the local supplement: On the 20th of this month, I read the cartoon "Recruiting Advertisements" published in your magazine, signed by Shao Xiang, and was extremely surprised. My name is Chen Shao Xiang. The cartoon published in your magazine was not made by me. How could it be published under my name? If there is the same name, the style of the signature is also very similar. It is suspected that a shameless person is taking the opportunity to obtain manuscript fees, but the original draft is also copied. Readers will inevitably add blame to each other. This is both fraudulently signing the artist's name and unreasonably damaging my reputation. The crime is heinous. Therefore, I especially ask you to publish the original letter for correction in order to avoid misunderstanding, and hope to reveal the address of the submitter to the public. It is what I hope for.

I wish you good health, Chen Shao Xiang

Novel

A Major Event in Wujia Town (6) 224

— Zhang Yiping

Lord Fu's wife's brother, Zhu Quangui, initially stood by Old Master Wu. He had accepted his sister's tearful plea and intended to say a few words of support today, because she only had her brother to rely on. Although women are often unreasonable, there had been many precedents for winning such cases in Wujia Town. Today, so many well-dressed relatives were gathered, and nine out of ten were speaking for Fusheng, so she heavily relied on her brother to help. However, the brother was not the sister. Seeing the menacing approach of Old Master Wu, he couldn't bear to suffer this immediate disadvantage, so he secretly slipped out of the vicinity and went to mingle with his two young nephews.

Lord Fu raised his head, his eyes still with that fierce, predatory gaze. He had another debt in his heart that he hadn't mentioned! The expenses for Fusheng's wedding had been forcibly included in the accounts by Old Master Wu. So, he steeled himself and said:

"Uncle, I have always acted fairly. My sister-in-law is a young widow, and Fusheng is my own son. However… there were two years of famine, the wartime events, and then the expenses of seeking refuge in Shanghai. This time, Fusheng's marriage has put me in debt."

Old Master Wu seemed to get angry, lightly tapping the rosewood table with his palm. Lord Fu hurriedly lowered his head, not understanding what he had said wrong, or even what he had said.

"Fu Ming, our Wu family cannot do such dishonorable things," the Old Master said without any courtesy, "You are someone who cares about face. If I have to examine the account books of past years, everyone will lose face!"

"Uncle, don't be angry…" Lord Fu didn't finish his sentence before a maid came out from the inner hall and said that the Madam had asked the Lord to come inside, which made Lord Fu even more anxious. He took a few steps without moving his feet, and finally scurried inside like a fleeing rabbit.

The small group immediately began to discuss the matter noisily, drowning out the sound of the cicadas being brought in. Old Master Wu patted Fusheng's shoulder, "As long as I, Old Master Wu, am here, I will never let you suffer." Zhang Defu chuckled, feeling that his plan had not failed.

Zhu Quingui and his two young nephews had slipped away unnoticed. The hall was almost entirely filled with the Fusheng faction. Zhang Defu was naturally the most active member. The two aunts and the aunt-in-law had long been displeased with Lord Fu's fear of his wife. Today, they braved the hot weather to come and prepare for a battle of words. But seeing Old Master Wu taking the lead and completely seizing victory, everyone wore triumphant smiles.
